The Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway's Motor Express Train Test Run Yesterday: Kowloon to Guangzhou in Two Hours and Fifteen Minutes Breaks the Far East Train Speed Record 31

(Guangzhou) The Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway's newly installed motor express train, the Taipo Queen, had a test run on the morning of the 14th. It departed from Kowloon at 7:45 AM and arrived in Guangzhou at 10:00 AM, taking a total of two hours and fifteen minutes, with an average speed of 79.45 kilometers per hour, breaking the Far East train speed record. The train car has a silver streamlined design, is approximately sixty feet long, ten feet wide, and fifteen feet high. The front is the engine room, the middle is the smoking room, and the rear is the seating area. There are a total of 24 seats, which are new-style sofas, luxurious and comfortable. Mr. Hawkes, the British section director of the railway, personally rode the train to the province. According to him, after consulting with Li Luchao, the Chinese section director, he plans to add another train to run between Guangzhou and Kowloon. The passenger fare is planned to be 12 yuan. Currently, the Guangzhou-Kowloon train takes two hours and fifty-five minutes for the entire journey. After the new train is put into operation, the connection between the province and Hong Kong will be closer. (Central News Agency dispatch, 14th)

Page 5

Current Affairs Commentary

The Issue of the Pacific Non-Fortification 55

— Lang

In the past month, the tension in Sino-Japanese relations has reached its highest point. Amidst this tense situation in the Far East, the issue of Pacific fortification has been raised again by Britain, sparking a major discussion between Japan and the United States. This is something that we should pay close attention to.

The so-called Pacific fortification issue originated from the Washington Conference. Because Article 19 of the Washington Naval Treaty stipulates that the UK, the US, and Japan must maintain the status quo on certain islands in the Western Pacific, and are not allowed to fortify them. These islands that are not allowed to be fortified include Guam, the Philippines, and the Aleutian Islands of the United States; Hong Kong and the islands east of the 110 degrees east longitude meridian in the Pacific (excluding Australia and New Zealand) of the United Kingdom; and the Kuril Islands, the Ogasawara Islands, the Amami Islands, the Ryukyu Islands, Taiwan, and Penghu of Japan. However, this Washington Naval Treaty will expire at the end of this year. Therefore, the British government proposed to Japan and the United States a few days ago to hold negotiations in the near future. Britain advocates that Article 19 should continue to be effective. The coastal defense and naval bases of all British, American, and Japanese territories in the Pacific should maintain the status quo in principle. However, existing defense works and naval bases that are outdated and inapplicable may be modified or renovated.

This proposal by Britain immediately aroused a strong reaction from the United States, which considered Britain's proposal to be an unfriendly attitude. Secretary of the Navy Swanson also issued a statement saying, "Military fortification must be met with military fortification. Threats must be met with threats." Why does the United States oppose the continuation of Article 19 of the treaty so strongly? This has historical reasons. Originally, the United States initially accepted the provisions restricting the fortification of Pacific islands on the condition that Japan respect China's territorial integrity, maintain the open door policy, and accept the 5:5:3 naval power ratio. Because only in a situation of equilibrium in the Far East would the United States not need to fortify the islands in the Western Pacific and establish naval bases to attack Japan. However, the situation has now completely changed. Japan has not only withdrawn from the naval conference and abandoned the 5:5:3 ratio agreement, but has also occupied our country's territory and undermined our country's sovereignty. At the same time, it has also damaged the interests of the United States in the Far East. Therefore, the United States must expand its navy and rebuild its naval bases in the Western Pacific in order to deal with Japan.

As for Japan's attitude, judging from its past stance, it should support Britain's proposal. Because the islands whose fortification is restricted are all in the Western Pacific. Therefore, it is very risky for Britain and the United States to cross the ocean to attack Japan. Although the islands near Japan are also restricted from fortification, this does not greatly harm Japan's interests. Therefore, when Japan withdrew from the London Naval Conference in the first half of the year, it still expressed its willingness to maintain the non-fortification provisions of Article 19 of the Sea Treaty. Although the Japanese Navy Ministry has recently expressed opposition to the previous restricted areas (i.e., referring to the Kuril Islands and other places very close to the Japanese mainland), this is just a show of force.

In this incident, the most peculiar thing is Britain's attitude. According to past relations and the situation of naval warfare, Britain should adopt the same attitude as the United States on the issue of fortification. Especially from the friendly relationship between Britain and the United States in recent years, and the British-Japanese strategic situation, Britain should not have made proposals that are beneficial to Japan. However, we know that British diplomacy has always been known for its cleverness. Perhaps this proposal is a gesture to exchange certain conditions with Japan.

Japanese Youth: Lowering the Military Service Age Under Consideration by Army and Navy Authorities 56

(Tokyo) It is reported that the issue of lowering the age for Japanese youth to serve in the army and navy is under consideration by the relevant authorities. Currently, the prescribed military service age in Japan is twenty years old, but it may be lowered to eighteen or nineteen years old. It is said that this proposal was put forward by the Ministry of Education, and the army and navy ministries are currently studying it. The benefits of lowering the military service age are approximately as follows: (1) to strengthen national defense, (2) to avoid interruptions in the careers of those enlisting, (3) to achieve social maturity earlier, and (4) to provide young people with more effective physical and mental training. According to those who support this plan, the Soviet Union announced in August of this year that it would reduce the compulsory military service age from twenty-one to nineteen. The reason the Soviet Union adopted this method is nothing more than to enable Soviet youth to obtain comprehensive physical development and to complete their military service early so that they can engage in various social occupations. According to the provisions of the Japanese Military Service Law, all healthy Japanese men between the ages of seventeen and forty should serve the country at any time when called upon by the state. However, in practice, physical examinations are only conducted at the age of twenty, and those who pass the examination are enlisted for service. Those who pass become active-duty soldiers, with a service period of one year and ten months for the army and three years for the navy. According to the Nichinichi Shimbun, approximately 850,000 young people are examined each year, of whom 85% are already employed, as most have been working since leaving school at the age of fourteen. At the age of twenty, it can be said that it is the most important period of life, because no matter what kind of work they are engaged in, their skills will inevitably undergo significant development at that time, and many people have to bear the economic responsibility of their families. Therefore, once enlisted, not only is their original career interrupted, but the lives of their families are also affected. Moreover, from the standpoint of national defense, the mechanization of modern armies and the increasing complexity of military strategies make it appropriate to start the training of soldiers earlier than currently stipulated. The Nichinichi Shimbun once published an argument that prolonged engagement in a certain occupation before enlistment often harms the intellect and comprehension of those enlisting, making it difficult for them to grasp the mysteries of military art. (Reuters, 14th)

Approaching Political Season: The Hirota Cabinet Faces Numerous Difficulties. Administrative Reform Issues Unlikely to Cause Fatal Wounds. Even If the Cabinet Changes, Its China Policy Will Ultimately Remain Unchanged. 57

(Tokyo) The Japanese political season has now arrived, and various difficult-to-handle political issues are awaiting resolution. Currently, all eyes are focused on the fate of the Hirota Cabinet. How can the unprecedentedly large budget of 3.2 billion for the next fiscal year be passed? How can the massive plan to increase taxes be accepted by the people? How can the state-run electricity scheme be implemented? How can the plan to reform the administrative structure be reconciled with reality? All of these are major difficulties for the Hirota Cabinet. Reducing the 3.2 billion budget is not permitted, so the burden on the people must be increased to make up for the shortfall. The recently announced planned tax increases have met with strong opposition, but there is a tendency to implement them. Regarding the electricity issue, the relevant authorities are currently drafting a compromise plan to satisfy the opposition of electricity entrepreneurs. This issue, like the budget and tax issues, is unlikely to cause a cabinet crisis, but it may become a difficult issue during the Diet session next spring. What requires extreme attention at present is the plan for reforming the administrative structure, which is firmly advocated by both the army and navy. The opposition points out that the plan will lead to the following results: (1) dictatorship, (2) wartime conditions, and (3) centralization. However, the supporters believe that the plan will strengthen the cabinet, make it easier to implement and unify national policies, and be unaffected by cabinet changes. The two sides seem likely to engage in heated debate. Because Prime Minister Hirota fears that the plan will not be easily passed, he does not want to implement it hastily, so it was not brought up for discussion at the cabinet meeting on the 13th. Furthermore, suggestions such as merging the various ministries of the cabinet and establishing ministers without portfolio would fundamentally transform the current cabinet. If these are realized, not only will the current cabinet members face the difficulty of deciding whether to stay or go, but also the actual effectiveness of the merger will be highly questionable. Today, it is rumored that Prime Minister Hirota plans to temporarily abolish the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, with its responsibilities to be divided between the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, and to appoint the current Minister of Colonial Affairs as a minister without portfolio to oversee all affairs currently under the four bureaus of investigation, resources, legislation, and statistics. Whether the above plan will be accepted by all parties is difficult to predict. According to observations by a special correspondent from the Central News Agency, the issue of administrative reform, although the most thorny of all issues, is unlikely to be a fatal blow to the current cabinet. Some compare the Hirota Cabinet to a rubber ball that is not easily broken. These words are indeed appropriate. All aspects of Japan believe that the Hirota Cabinet needs to exist. This view has not yet declined. Even those who drafted the administrative reform plan are unwilling to bear the responsibility of overthrowing the cabinet. Therefore, judging from the current situation, there is still much room for compromise. Some believe that the Japanese cabinet issue is closely related to China policy. However, it should be noted that even if the Hirota Cabinet falls, its successor, while perhaps making slight modifications to its China policy, will certainly make few changes to its general direction. If there are factors that can influence Japan's China policy, these factors are none other than whether China can truly unify and how international circumstances evolve. (Central News Agency, 14th)

Japanese Kamikawa Unit Suffers Heavy Losses

Upon hearing the news, the Japanese Izuka unit immediately dispatched a team to reinforce them. New Polish Political Party Advocates Bushido Spirit and Supports Democratic Rule 61

Warsaw A new Polish political party called the "Public National Camp" has the main characteristic that "all Poles from the age of six to sixty must join a semi-military organization." Italy Intensifies Naval and Air Force Preparations, Seeks Development in the Mediterranean, Thereby Protecting Significant Interests in Africa, British Naval Shift Eastward Arouses Fear 62

(Rome) The State Council recently issued a notice announcing that Italy should intensify military preparations in the near future. It is now known that the Italian government is particularly focused on the naval and air forces, and its attention is focused on the Mediterranean. Judging from the fact that the 1941 Italian International Exposition will be held in the port of Ostia (the port connecting Rome to the sea), it can be seen that the slogan adopted by the Italian government is indeed "developing from Rome towards the sea." The government now believes that the northeastern border has the Alps as a natural barrier, making it difficult for other countries to invade. The current army strength is sufficient to cope with any offensive. On the contrary, Italy, due to its geographical situation and its significant interests in Africa, urgently needs to have a strong navy to protect its coastlines. However, being equipped with only a navy is feared to be insufficient, and the government has decided to spend 140 million lire to build airfields along the coast to assist the navy. This is the main reason why the provincial government is expanding the naval and air forces. In addition, Italy's expansion of its navy has another reason, which is to target Britain. Historically, the British navy in the Mediterranean has used Malta as its main base, but it does not have a good base in the eastern Mediterranean. Malta is located a short distance from Italian territory. Recently, due to Italy's active preparations for military expansion, the position of the island has become threatened. After recently touring the Mediterranean, British First Lord of the Admiralty Hoare planned to build several bases in the eastern Mediterranean, further away from Italy, to form a complementary situation with Malta. The intention is not difficult to discern. In Italy, the right to freely travel through the eastern Mediterranean traffic routes is believed to be held by Italy in the future. Britain's naval shift eastward is naturally causing fear and trepidation. Therefore, after hearing about the policy Hoare intended to adopt, they were immediately shocked and wanted to reach a friendly compromise with that country. However, they were unwilling to express the word "compromise" orally or in writing. Therefore, they announced the expansion of the insulting army to signal Britain, so that they could pre-emptively secure their position for future negotiations. However, the real intention is not to compete with the British navy in the Mediterranean, because in terms of battleships, Italy currently has only four ships of 25,000 tons, excluding the two under construction (namely the "Vittorio Veneto" and "Littorio," each of 35,000 tons), among which only the "Caesar" and "Count Cavour" have been recently remodeled. In Britain, there are at least eight battleships that can be deployed. In comparison, Italy is inevitably dwarfed. However, Italy is far superior to Britain in terms of light warships. (Havas, 13th)

Germany Will Demand Revision of Anglo-German Naval Agreement, Believes Concessions to Russia Overthrow European Balance of Power, German Military Strategic Position Will Be Reconsidered 63

(Berlin) According to reliable sources here, the German government will soon ask the British government to revise the Anglo-German Naval Agreement as a result of the recent conclusion of the Anglo-Russian Naval Agreement. It is said that Hitler is currently discussing the issue with his cabinet members in his hometown of Bavaria. Upon investigation, the articles of the Anglo-German Naval Agreement of June 1935 did not have a final decision on the matter of revision. The agreement stated that only Britain could decide whether the actions of a third country should cause the overall situation to be reconsidered. However, the German government reserved the right to request Britain to consider the new situation if the general balance of naval armaments was drastically overthrown. Several German sources now insist that the Soviet Union's declaration in the Anglo-Russian Naval Agreement regarding its reservation concerning the status of its Far East navy and cruiser armaments has overthrown this balance. Germany believes that its military strategic position in the Baltic Sea will be greatly affected as a result. Currently, in the Anglo-German Agreement, the German naval armament ratio to Britain is 35 to 100, allowing for a fleet of only 400,000 tons, while the French fleet has 650,000 tons. The Germans view Russia's reservation as changing Germany's position at sea in the same way that they once pointed to the Franco-Russian military agreement as being sufficient to change Germany's military strategic position on land. It is worth recalling that when the Anglo-German Naval Agreement was signed, the newly appointed German Ambassador to Britain, General Ribbentrop, who signed on behalf of Germany, called it the first practical step towards arms limitation. Now, only sixteen months later, it has become a serious problem.

Russia and Germany Compete to Expand Navies, Germany Does Not Forget Old Territories, Propaganda Movement Enthusiastic 64

(Berlin) The propaganda movement to restore the old colonies before the European War has now spread throughout the country. The films shown in various cinemas mostly depict the beauty of the scenery of the old colony of Cameroon in Africa and the solid and lasting German construction projects. The shop windows in various bookstores are filled with books on colonial issues. The enthusiasm of German colonial sentiment is evident. (Havas, 14th)

Washington Publishes Secret Documents of the Paris Peace Conference, Proving that the United States Has No Ambition to Expand Overseas Territories, All Countries Should Enjoy Equal Business Opportunities in Former German Territories 65

(Washington) The U.S. State Department yesterday published the secret documents of the Paris Peace Conference regarding the disposition of German colonies. The detailed contents are translated as follows: These documents, mostly belonging to the U.S. foreign relations category of 1921, contain the U.S. government's advocacy that commercial opportunities in the mandated German colonies should be enjoyed equally by the people of all countries, and that the Allied countries should place the German colonies under international management. This full position caused severe disputes at that time in the correspondence between the U.S. and Allied diplomatic authorities. The most intense of these was the dispute between the United States and Japan over the issue of the U.S. mandate for the island of Yap in the Pacific. Yap Island is located between Guam and the Philippine Islands. President Wilson considered this island to be a key point for submarine telegraph cables and should be under international management to become a hub for world transportation. Japan, having obtained the mandate for this island and other islands north of the equator, vehemently opposed Wilson's proposal. Britain, bound by a secret treaty of 1916, spared no effort to support Japan. The United States was very angry at the time and stated in a document sent to Britain that the United States had made a strong contribution to the victory of the Allied countries in the war. In other words, if the United States had not assisted the Allied countries in winning the victory, how could Britain have had the right to dispose of the islands in the North Pacific? In fact, if the United States had not entered the war, the Allied countries would have had no hope of victory, and there would have been nothing to divide up. Now that the Allied countries have won the victory, the opportunity to dispose of the German colonies has arisen. All that the United States is asking for is equal opportunity related to its rights. If Britain is unable to assist the United States due to being bound by secret agreements, it should also notify the United States of the facts, and so on. The entire text proves that the United States has not demanded the expansion of its territory, but only demands that the people of all countries should enjoy equal business opportunities in the former German territories. (Kokumin News Agency, 13th)

Hitler Will Issue Important Declaration Clarifying Relations with France 66

Portugal Changes Punishment 68

Twenty-Eight Crew Members Sentenced to Imprisonment and Banishment

Lisbon After the crew members of the naval defense ship "Afonso de Albuquerque" and the destroyer "Dão" suddenly mutinied on September 8, the government sent troops to suppress them and arrested all the crew members and imprisoned them. The military special court interrogated them, and twenty-eight of them were sentenced yesterday. The lighter sentences were one year of imprisonment in a reformatory, and the heavier sentences were six years of imprisonment in a reformatory and ten years of banishment. However, those sentenced to one year of imprisonment in a reformatory can be changed to three years of banishment, and those sentenced to six years of imprisonment in a reformatory and ten years of banishment can be changed to twenty years of banishment. There are still sixty-three crew members who will continue to be interrogated today, and one hundred have been declared innocent and released because the evidence of their participation in the rebellion is not sufficient. US Ambassador to France Presents Credentials, US-Russian Diplomatic Relations Restored, Bullitt Played a Major Role 71

(Paris) - William Bullitt, the newly appointed US Ambassador to France, presented his credentials to French President Albert Lebrun today. Bullitt was the former US Ambassador to Russia, and the US recognition of Soviet Russia was almost entirely due to Bullitt's personal efforts. Bullitt is very wealthy. In 1919, President Wilson sent him to Soviet Russia to investigate the actual situation of the new Russian government. After returning to the United States, he strongly urged recognition. However, before Bullitt returned to the United States, President Wilson had discussed the Soviet Russian issue with Lloyd George, and his attitude changed, so he did not listen to Bullitt. At that time, Bullitt resigned himself. After Franklin Roosevelt took office in 1932, he brought up the Soviet Russian issue again, and Bullitt made a comeback. The following year, Bullitt attended the London Economic Conference and took the opportunity to discuss the restoration of US-Russian diplomatic relations with Soviet Foreign Minister Maxim Litvinov, which was a success. (National Telegraph dispatch, 13th)

(4) Congress has handed over the powers granted by the Constitution. Landon also stated that the government has used its huge propaganda machine to suppress criticism of the government. The southern wheat production report continued to be poor, causing the market price to rise, but later, the price fell slightly due to profit-taking, but the sentiment was still stable. At 1:00 PM, the October futures price was 8 shillings and 6.625 pence, which was 0.25 lower than yesterday's closing price.

Rubber

London - The rubber market is stable today. At 1:00 PM, the trading price for January-March futures was 8 pence exactly, which was the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York - The rubber market did not change at the opening this morning. Sentiment is still stable. It rose 1 to 2 points in the first hour. The New York commodity prices are listed on the left.

Japanese Army Urges Aviation Agreement, Japanese Planned Routes Include Five Provinces, Jinlian Aviation Has Already Been Opened Independently 78

Large-Scale Autumn Maneuvers by the Japanese Army in North China, Unprecedented Total Mobilization

Tianjin Correspondence, The Sino-Japanese aviation matter and the North China economic cooperation are the problems that the Japanese side values. Since the Japanese garrison in North China, led by Tadashiro, brought up the negotiation with Song Zheyuan in Tianjin on the 1st of this month when Song was in Tianjin, in order to achieve it urgently, they specifically ordered senior staff officer Iida Tsuchiyasu to visit Han in Jin again for further negotiations, and another staff officer, Wachi Takaeji, went to Ping with Songmuro to negotiate with Song again. Wachi himself had also visited Yan Xishan in Taiyuan to negotiate. The Japanese side hopes to open aviation routes in the five provinces of Hebei, Shanxi, Shandong, Chahar, and Suiyuan, following the example of the Eurasian and China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC), supervised by the Japanese military and operated by the Japanese-Manchukuo Aviation Company, and run a private organization. In addition to facilitating passengers and carrying mail, they also want to sign an agreement based on the negotiations between the former shareholders and the Japanese Kwantung Army's Yuguan Special Service Agency Chief Takeshita Yoshiharu before May 30th last year, repeating the old story. The Japanese planned routes are: (1) Jinlian, (2) Jinshen, (3) Pingcheng, (4) Chengbing, (5) Qinglian, (6) Shenji. These six routes are the main trunk lines, and there are several connecting lines in addition. The strength of the Hebei-Chahar authorities is only limited to Hebei and Chahar provinces, while the Japanese side's hope includes five provinces. This cannot be achieved by the Hebei-Chahar authorities directly agreeing to it. Therefore, the Japanese military's subordinates are dispatched separately to negotiate this matter, hoping to achieve it. However, since April of this year, the Japanese garrison in North China has independently opened Jinlian Aviation with four military aircraft. Every Monday and Thursday at 11:00 AM, they fly from Dalian to Tianjin and land at the CNAC airfield in Dongjuzi. At around 1:00 PM, they take off from Tianjin and return to Dalian. The aircraft numbers commonly seen are "27", "28", "125", and "125", all four monoplanes. The fare is 25 Japanese yen, which is cheaper than the second-class cabin of a Japanese mail ship between Tianjin and Dalian. However, non-military personnel who do not have a certificate are refused to board. The procedure for purchasing tickets is to obtain a certificate from the Japanese military in Tianjin and then purchase tickets from the Japanese garrison aviation department (also known as 口Public Hall) in the Japanese concession in Tianjin or the Dalian Aviation Branch, and then go to the airfield to board. Recently, the Japanese barracks in Dongjuzi, Tianjin, have been completed, and aircraft come and go from here, so very few outsiders know about it.

The autumn military exercise of the Japanese army in North China was originally scheduled to begin on October 20th. However, because the exercise plan was not completed by the Japanese military's operations section, and also because the communication battalion increased from Japan had not yet arrived to participate, it was postponed by one week and changed to start on October 25th and end on November 4th. The location is near Liangxiang, Changxindian, and Fengtai on the Pinghan Line. The participating troops are all Japanese garrisons stationed in North China, infantry, cavalry, artillery, engineering, and chemical special forces, all dispatched. From the 25th to the 28th, the exercise is held in regimental units. From the 29th to the 30th, the exercise is held in brigade units. From November 1st to the 4th, the exercise is a mixed division exercise, commanded by the first and second infantry regiments, Colonel Taguchi and Colonel Kayashima, and Infantry Brigade Commander Major General Kawabe. Japanese Commander Tadashiro will lead the military's staff to move to Changxindian on November 1st to set up a temporary command post there. All staff are assigned for wartime deployment. The air force under the command of Colonel 口Daiguchi in the aviation department in Tianjin will also lead two air force squadrons to participate. At that time, the air, land, cavalry, infantry, artillery, and chemical teams will maximize their functions to conduct exercises such as offense, defense, encounter, and night combat. The Japanese volunteer corps, retired soldiers, national defense foreign associations, and Boy Scout groups from all over North China will go to join the exercise from all over the country around the 28th. Therefore, the total number of mobilizations for this large-scale exercise is truly unprecedented. (13th)

Taiwanese Residents in Xiamen Killed, Japanese Police Illegally Arrested and Interrogated, Only Handed Over to the Public Security Bureau After Interrogation, Many Doubts Arise from the Autopsy of the Deceased 79

Xiamen Correspondence, The Japanese Consulate in Xiamen has a Japanese police station. However, the consulate is in the Gulangyu Concession, so the Japanese Consulate set up a Japanese police substation in the Xiamen urban area in our territory. This was originally not allowed by the treaty. The police powers exercised by the Japanese police substation are to manage Japanese and Taiwanese residents regarding police administration and judicial matters. However, regarding the execution of arrests, reports, and investigations, before September 18th, they would cooperate with our officialdom, or after our officialdom handled it, they would extradite it to the Japanese consulate. After September 18th, the entire matter was handled by the Japanese police station, and they directly executed it without cooperating with our officialdom. However, they have not yet overstepped their authority to apply it to our people. In August of this year, Ji from Tongan was arrested, claiming that he was Taiwanese, and he was released after being detained for ten days, which was the beginning of exceeding their authority. At 10:00 AM on the 10th of this month, the Japanese police substation suddenly reported that a Taiwanese woman named Zhu Chen, who lived at 193 Siming East Road, said that her husband, Taiwanese Zhu Chaoa, was selling noodles at the entrance of Zeng Guniang Lane. At 10:00 PM on the 7th, two people named Wu Fan Leng A ate noodles and paid, and a dispute arose over the authenticity of the banknotes. Zhu was beaten and injured, and died at 5:00 AM on the 10th. The police station immediately found out that Wu Fan was named Wei Zhaoyu, from Jinjiang, and Leng A was named Jiang Ling, from Hui'an, and were partners in Xingmao Foreign Firm on Jukou Street. The Japanese police were immediately dispatched to the foreign firm to arrest the two and interrogated them strictly. The two admitted that they had an argument with Zhu that night and did not admit to beating him to death. The Japanese police station immediately moved Zhu's body to the Japanese Boai Hospital in Gulangyu for an autopsy. At the same time, the Public Security Bureau was notified by telephone to inform the local court. The court inspector Xu Shaoxue and the Public Security Bureau's Judicial Section Xu Zongyue, led the director of Zhongshan Hospital's medical affairs, Zhang Maolin, to participate in the autopsy. As a result, the Japanese doctor Deng Ming diagnosed that the abdomen was beaten, causing a hole in the large intestine, leakage of excrement, and peritonitis leading to death. According to Dr. Zhang Maolin's judgment, if the deceased's stomach and intestines were ruptured by beating, he should have died immediately and could not have lasted for four days. As for the arrested Wei and Jiang, after being sent to the Xiamen Public Security Bureau by the Japanese Consulate, they will be presented for negotiation. It is found that this case was not reported to the police at the time of the fight, and after death for four days, it was not reported to the police and the court. There was no case before or after. The Japanese police station, according to the report, directly arrested our people and only sent them to our officialdom after interrogation. It is already overstepping its authority, and there are many doubts. Even Zhu Chaoa did not register with our officialdom as a Taiwanese. (October 14th)

Kunshan 80

County Government Reorganizes Cooperatives

There are a total of 118 cooperatives in this county. Most of them are loosely organized and their affairs are stagnant. Since the former cooperative instructor Qian Zongzhou was removed from his post due to a case, his successor, Shen Guixiang, found it difficult to start reorganizing them for a while. County Magistrate Peng had drafted improvement measures and implemented them step by step in the hope of gradually achieving perfection. Now, in order to thoroughly reorganize them, the county government has specially re-registered all the cooperatives in the county. Once completed, it will actively proceed according to the planned plan.

All Circles Form Joint Office

The county government believes that in this extraordinary period, all agencies and groups should earnestly prepare for contact and preparation. It has specially convened a meeting of all circles and gentry to decide to organize a joint office first and immediately start to prepare for its establishment.

Suzhou 81

Request to Reduce Tax Rate on Bamboo Sugar Industry

The Wu County Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Ministry of Finance on the 14th, stating that according to the statements of the Bamboo Industry Union and the Goods Industry Union, the business tax rate for each industry's bamboo sugar has always been 2 per mille, but it has now been increased to 5 per mille. At this time of commercial decline, the sharp increase in the tax rate is truly unbearable. They request a review and reduction, and that it still be collected at 2 per mille to reduce the burden on merchants.

Distribution of Push and Inspection Officers to Various Counties

The Jiangsu Higher Court, pursuant to the order of the Ministry of Judicial Administration to send each official who pushes and inspects out, has immediately distributed them for use. President Zhu and Chief Prosecutor Sun have already jointly distributed them. Eleven people have been assigned, including Jiangsu Higher Court Judge Zhu Yingrui, Gao Liqin, Wang Yuxiu, Wu County Local Court Judge Du Zuomin, Shanghai Local Court Judge Liu Baijun, Tang Youhua, Chen Pin, Cheng Weicheng, Yu Shiqi, Wang Yijun, Prosecutor Hu Songshu, Ma Weiqi, Wang Jiamen, Tongshan Local Court Judge Chen Sizhe, Songjiang Local Court Judge Chu Changhong, Jiangdu Local Court Judge Wang Ruyi, who have all gone to the Higher Court to thank the commission and take office. As for the Seventh Jiangsu Prison in Donghai, it has already been completed and established, and the ministry has appointed Wang Qi as the warden.

Wuxi 82

Terrible Tragedy of the Collapsed Great World

At 5 p.m. on the 13th, the parrot hall of the Great World Amusement Park outside Guangfu Gate on Dongxin Road in our county suddenly collapsed, injuring nineteen spectators. It is learned that the park was funded and opened by Li Xingru, Li Hanxiang, and others around March of the lunar calendar this year. The park site utilizes the old Qingsheng Theater on Dongxin Road and the remaining land of the Shengwen Cemetery for construction. It was completed and opened on the Dragon Boat Festival. In addition to the Qingsheng Theater performing Peking Opera, there are also the Phoenix, Partridge, Peacock, and Parrot halls, which respectively perform song and dance, drama, Suzhou Tanci (storytelling and ballad singing), a gathering of beautiful women, Wuxi local opera, Yangzhou opera, and a variety of comical acts. At the beginning of the opening, people from the general lower and middle classes of society flocked to it, and business was booming. However, the buildings in each part of the park were built hastily due to the short time, and the construction was inevitably sloppy. Recently, as the weather has turned cooler in autumn, the Parrot Hall has been renovated to perform elegant storytelling sessions with a gathering of famous artists from Suzhou. The Puyu Society Tanci artists Guang Yaozhang, his daughters Lifang and Lijuan, as well as Wang Tingsun, Qian Yunpeng, Zhu Chengtian, and others were hired to perform day and night the stories of "Three Smiles," "The Case of Peng Gong," "The Five Righteous Men," "Green Peony," "The Contract," "Kunshan Ji," and others. At 5 p.m. on the afternoon of the 13th, when the Zhang father and daughters finished singing the opening piece "Daiyu Burning the Manuscript," and were about to continue with the Kunshan Ji, with a crash, the entire building suddenly collapsed. The Zhang father and daughters were unable to escape and were both injured. At the same time, thirty or forty audience members in the hall were also crushed under the rubble and tiles. A total of nineteen people were injured, all with head injuries and bleeding. For a time, the hall was noisy and chaotic. Later, the staff of the park carried the injured to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Among them, Huang Lifang, Wang Zhoushi, Lu Danshi, Ni Qingyu, Zou Jinbao, and Sun Rongxian were the most seriously injured, and it is feared that they will become disabled. After receiving the news, Zhang Da, the head of the Public Security Bureau, immediately dispatched Huang Erheng, the captain of the patrol team, and Fang Henian, an inspector, leading more than ten members of the patrol team to the Great World to investigate, and brought Xie Li, Li Han, to the bureau for investigation. Yesterday, the 14th, the park operated as usual, but the audience was sparse. It is said that the county government, considering the poor construction of the park, will order the Public Security and Construction Bureaus to take measures to ban it in order to avoid danger.

Establishing a Model Silk Factory

The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province, in view of the developed sericulture and numerous silk factories in our county, but not much attention being paid to silk reeling techniques and research, resulting in products that cannot compete with Japanese silk, is planning to establish a Wuxi Model Silk Factory. Tang Xixiang, director of the Hangzhou branch of the Sericulture Improvement Association, has been appointed concurrently as the director of the preparatory office of the Model Silk Factory. After Tang accepted the appointment, he immediately began preparations, advocating emphasis on the experimentation of reeling and the research of new technologies. The initial establishment expenses are tentatively set at 170,000 yuan. The provincial government has now approved the allocation of 100,000 yuan in one lump sum, with the remainder to be paid successively. The location has been selected next to the silk cocoon testing department of the Qianqiao Sericulture Testing Ground, covering an area of more than 20 mu. Construction will begin this winter and is scheduled to be completed next spring. The building style will be entirely Japanese. The factory's mechanical equipment will be planned by the silk reeling expert Zou Jingheng. The silk reeling machines will all use Japanese-style twenty-eye oscillating machines, initially fifty units, and a testing department will be set up separately, equipped with more than twenty types of new and unique silk reeling machines, including Italian machines (old style), Japanese oscillating machines (new style), and multi-end machines (the latest style), with two units of each type, totaling more than fifty units. After its establishment, young, literate women will be recruited to engage in training in silk reeling techniques, with higher compensation than ordinary workers. Food and lodging will be provided by the factory, and special attention will be paid to hygiene facilities, so that all will serve as a model for other silk factories. The preparatory office is located in the Sericulture Testing Ground and is temporarily divided into two departments: technical and sanitary affairs. Technical matters are the responsibility of Zou Jingheng and Zou Haiquan, while several clerks are hired for administrative matters. Currently, the sample hall is expected to issue drawings and begin preparations within days.

Changshan 83

The Entire Family of the Baozhang (Neighborhood Head) Was Brutally Murdered

The area of Fangcun Jinyuan Furong in Changshan is mountainous, transportation is difficult, and the place is developing rapidly. Suichang was twice occupied by bandits in August. Recently, they have become even more rampant, looting, burning, and killing, happening several times a day. The residences of the Baozhang in Furong Xiyuan Township have all been burned. Wang Jinliang, the Baozhang of Yuanyuan, was killed along with his entire family. The local donations were not rewarded, and the number of men and women killed was also over thirty. Local residents leave their villages every night and spend the night on the mountain peaks, a very miserable situation.

Changshu 84

All the Prisoners Went on a Hunger Strike

All the prisoners in the county prison here staged a hunger strike on the morning of the 13th. It is said that the reason was the authorities' reduction of prisoner rations. According to regulations, each prisoner's ration is 25 taels per serving, except for those who contract for their own meals from outside. However, since Gong Yuanbin took over as director of the prison in our county, he has been concerned that the monthly rations are often insufficient due to the large number of detainees. Therefore, as a cost-cutting measure, he deducted five taels from each prisoner's ration, actually issuing twenty taels. As a result, the prisoners suddenly saw their rations reduced and were unable to fill their stomachs. They requested Director Gong to restore the previous situation, but he ignored them. Therefore, the prisoners agreed to go on a hunger strike on the 13th to protest. The prison staff tried hard to persuade them, but the prisoners remained adamant. By 2 p.m., the matter had not been resolved. As a result, it was agreed that the rations would be slightly increased from the 14th and weighed on a market scale before each meal, which resolved the situation.

Prolonged Drought Damaged Late Rice

For a month, it has not rained, and the weather has been unusually dry. Many people in society have suffered from throat diseases and malaria. Moreover, the late rice planted in the Meitang area has not yet fully matured and grown, and needs to be soaked in rainwater. Because it has not rained for a long time, coupled with the scorching sun, most of the late rice has withered and died, and the soil is as hard as iron. Even if water is pumped, it will be of no use. Therefore, the farmers are quite worried.

Zhenjiang 85

Major Fire on the Riverside of Zhonghua Road

Around 1 a.m. on the 13th, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen behind the Huayang Building on the riverside of Zhonghua Road due to carelessness. At that time, the north wind was very strong, and the location of the fire was facing the Yangtze River, so the wind was even stronger. As a result, the fire spread to Shun Chang Hardware Store, Yingbin Hotel, Chuntai Hotel, Fuyun Steamship Bureau, and about a dozen nearby tofu and noodle shops, as well as shacks. The three-story building of the Beautiful Western Restaurant across the street was also affected. Fortunately, public security fire trucks and fire brigades from various sections rushed to the scene after hearing the news and tried their best to put out the fire. It was not until about 2 a.m. that the fire was extinguished. Wang Guisheng, the manager of the Huayang Building, where the fire started, was taken to the fourth sub-bureau of the first branch for interrogation and punishment. It is reported that the fire destroyed thirty-two houses, causing a loss of about forty to fifty thousand yuan.

Yangzhou 86

Auditor Sent to Audit Accounts

The Department of Finance recently sent auditor Guo Xiangzhi to Yangzhou to audit the accounts receivable and payable of various agencies related to the county treasury. Yesterday, accompanied by Liu Shixiang, director of the county accounting office, he went to the county government's property department and the Public Security Bureau to audit for a long time and gave many instructions. It is said that he will stay in Yangzhou for another day or two. Once the work is completed, he will go to the Gao Shi area to audit.

Bandits Robbed Remittance Letter

Jiang Hanbo, the accountant of the Jiangdu County Government, was traveling by car near the Fifth Lane of the Old City around 12 p.m. on the 13th when he caught sight of two men in long gowns and leather shoes running towards him. They brushed past his car and disappeared. Soon after, another person, also panting and sweating, came tracking after them. Surprised, Jiang asked what was happening. The man said his name was Wang Yuanzhang and he was a clerk at the Jiangsu Bank in the city. Zhou Houjun, the director of the Jiangsu Bank in Guanyun, had remitted ten yuan to the home of Zhou Xianglin at No. 24 Dongguan Street. Wang had been ordered to deliver the money to Zhou's house and a letter to the county education bureau. When he arrived at Zhou's house, only a doorkeeper was there, so he took the money back, asking her to tell her master to come to the bank to collect the money. Afterward, he went to the county government to deliver the official letter, intending to go to the education bureau afterward. However, when he walked to the entrance of the Fifth Lane of the Old City, three men in long gowns and leather shoes suddenly appeared, ordering him to stop, swarming forward, searching him, and robbing the ten yuan remittance before running away. Only then did he realize that they were bandits. Jiang was shocked to hear that a robbery had occurred near the county government in broad daylight. He immediately reported to County Magistrate Ma, who ordered the police chief Shi of the third branch of the Public Security Bureau and Liu Zonghan of the detective team to solve the case within a time limit.

Nantong 87

Dong Huibo Escorted to Nantong by Sea

Dong Huibo, the former commander of the Jiangsu Province Sea Guerrilla Force, was arrested for extortion in Haimen County. The Fourth District Security Command, considering Dong's serious crimes, ordered County Magistrate Chen of Haimen to escort him to Nantong. He was escorted there on the 13th, interrogated by Judge Chu, and then detained.

Suppressing Bandits in Rugao and Taixing

In the areas bordering Rugao and Taixing, bandits have recently gathered and are very rampant, having spread to Jingjiang. Wan Tan, the commander of the Fourth District Security Command, sent people to investigate and drafted a suppression plan, which was approved by the provincial authorities. Deputy Commander Peng Longxiang was sent to supervise the suppression and set up a command post in Huangqiao, planning to suppress the bandits and take over the Qingxiang within the shortest possible time.

Ningbo 88

Wealthy Businessman from Fenghua Kidnapped

Mao Junyi, a wealthy businessman from Yantou Village, Xianxiao Township, Fenghua, who possessed a large fortune, was targeted by bandits in the fourth year of the Republic of China and had already been kidnapped once, but luckily escaped. Afterward, he moved to Ningbo and opened the Rencheng firewood store on Haohe Street, and was also a shareholder of the Taichang woodenware store on Nanjing Road in Shanghai. This time, he returned to his hometown to arrange a burial site for his deceased wife, and was discovered by bandits. Suddenly, around 12 p.m. on the 9th, they gathered thirty or so bandits, each holding guns, broke into Mao's residence, dragged Mao out of bed, and kidnapped him. Before leaving, they fired guns to intimidate and left a letter demanding $185,000 in foreign currency. The military doctors are currently searching for them.

A Glimpse of Changxindian (Special Dispatch from Beiping) 89

The exercise grounds for our garrison used to be located in Miaojiadi, near the suburbs of Beiping. At that time, it was called "Target Practice." Later, the scale expanded, and the name changed to "Exercise." And the location extended from the suburbs to Fengtai. Later, the scale became even larger, extending westward from Fengtai to Lugouqiao and Changxindian on the Pinghan Line. Thus, in addition to exercises, there were also so-called "Marches" and so-called "Camping." Recently, the date for the large-scale "Autumn Maneuvers" has been formally notified to us, and the area will be further expanded southward, including Liangxiang County as well. I once read an essay by the Japanese essayist Yūsuke Tsurumi. In it, upon hearing the rumbling of cannons from Changxindian in Beijing, he expressed his infinite sadness at the revolving-lantern-like civil wars of the Feng-Zhili warlords in China at that time. More than ten years later, although the sound of cannons can be heard again, its meaning is completely different from the past. I wonder what Mr. Tsurumi would think if he heard it now.

At 2 p.m., the reporter took the No. 43 ordinary passenger train from Beiping to Changxindian. The journey took a total of 50 minutes. The scenery along the way was pleasant. After leaving Xibianmen, vegetable plots and nurseries were all green, stretching for about ten miles. On the green fields, there were one or two red or white horses, dotting the landscape, all turning water wheels to irrigate the plots. Farmers in the villages were bending over in the fields, busy working. When the train passed, they all shielded their eyes with their hands and looked up. The quiet and peaceful atmosphere made one feel as if they were in a painting. Imagining it, the sound of cannons and gunfire from dozens of miles away, to them, must sound like firecrackers, and they must constantly be suspicious, perhaps wondering why there were so many weddings far away. The more I think about it, the more I sigh. Not much sorghum was seen along the way, but peanuts, soybeans, and the like were everywhere. There were also many coal shops and steam furnace shops near the railway. For dozens of miles, the train passed several coal trains with ten or more cars. The abundance of coal produced along the Pinghan Line is evident. All of the above are very different from the various scenes along the Beining Road to Fengtai. And what makes one feel more at ease than between Ping and Fengtai is two things. First, the advertising signs for a certain foreign product have slightly decreased, and second, the tracks of certain foreign vagrants are also rarely seen. At least in the current situation, the control of a certain country over this road is indeed slightly less than its control over the Beining Road.

As the train approached Changxindian, just as the reporter was looking north out the window, he suddenly heard a fellow passenger shouting repeatedly, "Look! Look! Look! Look!" Turning around quickly and looking south out the window, he saw foreign troops lined up in seven or eight rows at the foot of the distant mountains and on the winding road, heading northwest. The place was exactly the road between Lugouqiao and Changxindian, and at that time, they were heading from Lugouqiao to Changxindian. A farmer-like passenger suddenly asked the reporter, "Why are they all ×× soldiers! Where are our own?" The reporter had no words to answer and could only force a wry smile. But he did not give up his question, and pressed the reporter even harder. "Sir! Sir! Hmm? Hmm?" At this time, the reporter felt extremely embarrassed. Fortunately, he suddenly pointed out the window and shouted loudly to himself, "Look, look! On that hilltop, look: isn't that our team!" The reporter followed his finger and looked, and as a result, he recognized that the team standing on the hilltop was still in khaki uniforms, not the gray ones of our own army. I suppose the reporter's eyesight was slightly better than this honest farmer. But in order not to disappoint him too much, I couldn't bear to break the news.

At 2:50 p.m., the train arrived at Changxindian Station. The first thing that caught my eye was the station sign. Unlike the Beining Road, the station name did not include any foreign writing in addition to the Chinese and English station names. Next to the Chinese characters was the National Phonetic Alphabet. From afar, I suspected it was foreign writing. Looking closely, I realized it was the phonetic alphabet, and the feeling of gratification was, as people usually say, "indescribable."

Exiting the station and entering the streets of Changxindian. This is a town belonging to Wanping County. The street is an east-west street, and the households face each other from north to south across the street. The street is about four or five miles long, with about a thousand households. In a small alley on the east side of the street, near the station, there is a post office. Apart from everything else that is common elsewhere, there is a long strip of paper specially posted at its entrance, reading "Agency for Exchanging Central China Communications Bank Legal Tender." Seeing this also gave me an inexplicable feeling of gratification. At the east end of the street, there is a primary school, and the town chief's office is also attached to it. The eastern section of the street is a dirt road, the middle section is cobblestones, and the western section is also a dirt road, all about a few dozen feet wide. On both sides of the street center, there are shallow ditches, with no standing water. Between the ditch and the front of the households, there is a raised space of about two feet. Occasionally, there are food stalls, but most of them are filled with men, women, old and young, chatting and passing the time, their attitude very leisurely. Pedestrians on the street are sparse, and a dozen camels carrying sacks are actually lying in the center of the street to rest, blocking the road, but the townspeople seem to be used to it and do not find it strange at all. Rickshaw pullers also have no customers to pull, leaning idly on the rickshaw handles, or dozing off, or reading tabloids, or smoking cigarettes, everywhere. The slanting rays of the early autumn sun highlight a scene of leisure and relaxation.

Statistically, among the shops along the street, general stores are the most numerous, followed by tea and pastry shops. Other types of shops, such as barber shops, restaurants, and clothing stores, which are common everywhere in large cities, are rarely seen here. This is due to the different needs. The wind of economic depression has also spread to this small town. Signs for big discounts and big giveaways flutter in the wind outside the dilapidated storefronts. But in reality, not only are there no customers, but there are not many people walking on the street.

Advertising for foreign goods such as Lao Du eye drops and Daxue eye drops is also rare between the walls, but much less than in Fengtai and other places. Especially advertisements for domestic goods, such as Great Wall cigarettes, Beauty cigarettes, and even Two Girls brand old-fashioned cologne, also appear on the walls from time to time, which is completely absent in places like Fengtai. The most striking thing along the street is the advertising signs for Daxue eye drops and Lao Du eye drops erected outside the doors of the grocery stores. The signs are four or five feet high, with a half-length portrait of a foreign old man painted at the top. Roughly calculated, there are about a dozen such advertising signs in the entire Changxindian street, which can also be said to be quite a few.

In the middle of the street, there is a private middle school converted from a temple. The facade is dilapidated, with the school sign "Private Wenyi Middle School" and the horizontal inscription "Fairy Temple" side by side. Outside the door, three or four beggar-like people are sitting and scratching themselves in the sun. Entering is a corridor, at the end of which is a magnificent hall, already in disrepair. A ten-foot-high iron tripod is placed in front of the hall. As the reporter wandered under it, the students in the classrooms on both sides stretched their heads out of the windows in clusters and looked at the reporter from afar, whispering in each other's ears, not knowing what they were saying. It is not easy to concentrate on classes in this environment.

On the hill opposite the station, there is a school for the children of railway employees. The building is neat and the layout is elegant. Looking down from the hill, the scenery within a radius of more than ten miles is all within sight. At that time, they were having a music lesson, and the singing was loud and majestic, spreading from the hill, filling the valley and the sidewalks. What they were singing was the Song of the Broad Road. At 5:18 p.m., the No. 42 train moved north towards Beiping. Although there was constant gunfire coming from the northeast, the majestic singing on the hillside was also quite loud, which inspired infinite enthusiasm in the midst of sadness. (11th)

Educational News

The Status of Private Schools in Various Provinces and Cities Across the Country 90

The Ministry of Education recently compiled the following overview of private schools in various provinces and cities across the country in the 24th year:

(Notes) (1) It is claimed that since the 22nd year, all private schools in Xinjiang Province have been taken over by the cultural promotion associations of various ethnic groups and converted into association-established elementary schools, and there are few remaining. Weihaiwei reported that there are currently no private schools in its territory. Hunan and Xikang provinces have not submitted reports and are therefore omitted. (2) Most of the counties and cities under the jurisdiction of each province have not been able to submit complete reports. For example, in Jiangxi, Hubei, Yunnan, Shandong, Sichuan, Guizhou and other provinces, more than half or nearly one-third have failed to submit reports. According to the simplified administrative region table published by the Ministry of Internal Affairs, these 22 provinces (including Xinjiang) have more than 1,680 counties and cities. Currently, reports have been submitted by approximately 1,300 counties and cities (of which approximately 330 counties and cities have reported no private schools), accounting for approximately 82% of all counties and cities. (3) Among the 100,000+ private schools, approximately 35,304 have been improved (using school textbooks), and 65,630 have not been improved (not using school textbooks). Among the provinces and cities with improved schools, Shanghai accounts for the most at 92.77%, and Chahar accounts for the most at 8.66%. Qinghai has no improved schools. Jiangsu has the most at 20,000+ schools, and Qinghai has the fewest at only eight schools. (4) There are 31,037 improved tutors and 65,776 unimproved tutors. Among the 100,000+ tutors, 8,533 have received normal school education, 21,621 have received primary and secondary school education, and 70,659 are from private schools. Among the provinces and cities with teachers who have received normal school education, Shanxi has the most, accounting for 28.02%, and Zhejiang has the least, accounting for 3.06%. (5) Among the 1.7 million+ students, 708,556 are improved and 1,048,458 are not improved. Among the provinces and cities with improved students, Shanghai accounts for the most at 93.90%, while Guangxi accounts for 81.34%. Chahar has the fewest at 13.05%. On average, each private school has 18.09 students. Qinghai and Nanjing have the most at 25.38 students per school, while Shandong has the fewest at 11.2 students. (6) The annual tuition collected is 6,557,733 yuan. On average, each private school collects approximately 64 yuan, 80 cents in tuition. Beijing collects the most on average at 173 yuan. Most cities collect over 100 yuan. Among the provinces, only Guangdong collects 111 yuan per year, and most are between 40 and 70 yuan. The average annual tuition fee is 3 yuan, 58 cents. Qingdao has the highest average at 13 yuan, 60 cents per student, and most are only between 3 and 6 yuan. Qinghai has only 1 yuan, 80 cents, and Gansu has the lowest at 1 yuan, 70 cents. (7) The number of private schools is approximately one-third of the number of elementary schools, the number of private school teachers is approximately one-sixth of the number of elementary school teachers and staff, but the number of students taught is very large. At this time of promoting compulsory education, the reorganization and improvement of private schools so that management, training and teaching can be gradually improved, and the selection of excellent ones to be converted into short and small primary schools, is of great help to the future of compulsory education.

Dr. Xue Guangqian's Speech: The Revival of Italy and China (Part 1) 96

Because the Party Serves the People, the People Love the Party Unswervingly; Reviving China Requires No Theory, but Speaking the Truth and Doing Real Things

The city's Banking Association held a lecture yesterday afternoon at 6:00 PM at the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road, inviting Dr. Xue Guangqian to speak on "The Revival of Italy and China." More than 300 people attended. The main points of his speech are recorded below. Ladies and gentlemen, today's lecture topic is "The Revival of Italy and China." The reason for discussing the way to revive China with Italy as a backdrop is not because Italy is the strongest, wealthiest, and most advanced country today. It is because, 14 years ago, Italy was still a country full of scars and riddled with holes. Since Mussolini came to power, he has been striving for good governance, and the country's power has been growing day by day. The way he reformed and built the country has many aspects that can be learned from by our countrymen. Moreover, its people inherited the legacy of the Roman Empire and became old and backward, just like China today. Its national political system is also similar to one-party rule. Therefore, its national character and conditions are different from those of European and American countries. To discuss the success of Italy's one-party rule, we must explore its

Party and Government Organization

The structure of the organization: The Italian people are rich in loyalty to the monarch. Therefore, although the Fascist Party holds power, it still sets up a nominal monarch and does not abolish it. The government organization is based on party laws and various other laws. The Fascist Party believes that to maintain the authority of party governance, it must absolutely not relax its grip on political power. It uses the power of the party to infiltrate the government organization, so that there is no boundary between party and government, and they are integrated. For example, newspaper censorship does not involve setting up another agency in the central party headquarters, but rather adding a propaganda department to the cabinet, alongside the Ministry of the Interior and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and having it presided over by party members. This makes the public see that the censors are not the party headquarters but the government. All government words and deeds are based solely on the law. Laws are all implemented through decrees, so the public believes that the censors are actually acting on imperial will. There is no time to obey imperial will, so how can there be any reason to rebel? Youth training is also the most important task of the party, but it does not involve setting up a special agency in the central party headquarters to take charge of it. Instead, a Deputy Minister of Physical Education is added to the Ministry of Education to implement training according to the party constitution. However, the public sees that the youth trainers are not the party headquarters but the government and the monarch. As for the

Party's Work

It is entirely a social relief undertaking. Public officials throughout Italy are given priority to party members when hired (currently, recruitment of party members has been suspended; there are now two methods for joining: one is to receive party training from birth until the age of 21 before being allowed to join, and the other is for university students under the age of 26 to join the university's Fascist group and be accepted only after two years). Therefore, no party members are unemployed. As a result, the party headquarters are closed during the day, and the party congress is held once a year and is very simple, reporting on the financial situation of the past year. The usual activities are all after 8:00 PM. The party headquarters are similar to a club, with a cafe, dance hall, reading room, and music room, becoming a place for leisure after work. All work is centered on providing relief to the poor in the district, and decisions are made during these after-dinner conversations. Therefore, saying that there are no meetings is actually equivalent to a major gathering. As for the source of funds, it mostly comes from party members. Therefore, the Fascist Party of Italy not only has party members supporting the party, but also takes care of the poor. Because the party can serve the people, the people love the party and do not waver in their loyalty to the party. Another important task of the party is the unified control of work and leisure time. Because Italy was plagued by communist disturbances before Mussolini came to power, great attention was paid to the lives of workers. After the workers' eight-hour workday, the party headquarters formulated various methods to organize and control their leisure time, so that they could not and would not want to get close to the communists. If various sports competitions are held, they can not only cultivate their minds and bodies but also lead them onto the right track and enjoy legitimate entertainment. However, throughout the country, there are no slogans or banners of support or opposition. When I visited Italy, it was when the Italo-Ethiopian War broke out, so I witnessed firsthand how it coped with economic sanctions and ultimately achieved victory. Italy's invasion of Ethiopia had been planned for a long time, so its launch was not triggered by a sudden impulse, and its victory was not achieved overnight.

Shanghai YMCA Painting and Map Competition 97

Registration begins today; competition to be held on the 22nd of next month.

Cash and books awarded to the top 30 finishers. The Shanghai YMCA, in order to encourage promising young people to become familiar with the geography of their country, has initiated a map painting competition. The detailed rules have been decided at the second committee meeting and are recorded below.

Registration and Participation: All citizens of the Republic of China between the ages of 15 and 25, regardless of gender, are eligible to register and participate, limited to residents of Shanghai. Registration forms can be obtained from the YMCA office starting today, filled out, and submitted with a registration fee of one silver dollar to show seriousness.

Competition Rules: (A) Draw a full map of the country. (1) You may refer to the latest published map of China from various police stations. (2) The content must include provinces, railways, major rivers, important cities, and indicate the main products of each province. (3) A specified sheet of paper will be issued by the YMCA at the time of registration for drawing. The drawing must be submitted to the YMCA at the time of the silent map competition, with the name, age, and a statement that it is the participant's own work. (B) Silent map competition. (1) All registered participants must come to the YMCA at 9:00 AM on November 22 (Sunday) to draw silently (if there are many students participating in one school, it can be held separately within the school). (2) The YMCA will issue a specially made blank map of the country. (1) The names of the provinces, important cities, and major railways are marked, and the participant can draw in detail one or several provinces based on his personal point of view, considering the political center, transportation hub, or national defense center of the country.

Judging Criteria: (A) (1) Accuracy, (2) Importance, (3) Neatness, (4) Completeness, (B) The score of the silently drawn blank map of the country accounts for 60%, and the score of the full map of the country accounts for 40%. Chairman of the competition judging committee: Tan Lian, Vice Chairman: Li Changchuan, Committee members: Chen Duo, Hong Mao Xi, Huang Jingwan, Ge Suicheng, Chu Zeng, Chu Shaotang, Su Jiarong, Chen Queji, Gu Yinming, Dong Wen, Ding Shaohuan, Tu Encong, Yang Huaiseng, Tian Xingeng, Tu Wei.

Awards: In order to encourage participation and increase interest in the competition, the awards are set as follows: First place: 30 yuan, Second place: 20 yuan, Third place: 15 yuan, Fourth place: 10 yuan, Fifth place: 5 yuan, Sixth to tenth place: 3 yuan, Eleventh to thirtieth place: Books will be awarded. All participants will be given a commemorative medal as a souvenir.

City North School Restores Business Courses 98

Private Shanghai City North Middle School has been established for more than 20 years and has always been divided into high school and junior high school. The high school is further divided into liberal arts and business courses. Due to the destruction of the school building during the January 28 Incident, the business courses were temporarily suspended. Now that the school building has been rebuilt and is even more expanded than before, and in order to promote vocational education to meet the needs, the vocational courses will be restored starting next semester. The Senior Accounting Department will be established first, and it has been submitted to the Shanghai Education Bureau to forward to the Ministry of Education for instructions. After receiving the Ministry's order, the school first established a vocational course preparatory committee, recommending Dr. Xu Peikun, former President of the National Business College, as the director of the preparatory committee. At the same time, Xu Yongzuo, Pan Xulun, Jin Guobao, Wang Zhicui, Zhou Yangwen, Xu Peikun, Lin Jinyu, Pan Zhongjia, Yang Weiyu, Pan Yangyao, and Zhuang Zhujiu and other experts were invited as consultants. It was established the other day, and Xu Yongzuo was elected as the chairman of the consultant committee to discuss all implementation methods.

Tilden Arrives in Shanghai; Performance Program Under Discussion; Tilden Wrote Yesterday Saying He Will Perform Five Sets of Singles with Vines; Canavaro Asks to Partner with Mecca Again for a Doubles Performance 99

The world professional tennis players Tilden, Vines, and Miss Sharbo and their party, after deciding to pass through Shanghai on the 6th of next month to attend the performance, everything has become a reality. What everyone wants to know most now is the program of the performance. According to Mr. Canavaro, who is in charge of this competition, Mr. Tilden sent him a letter yesterday (the 13th), saying that he has decided to perform a singles match with Vines, with a total of five sets. Mr. Canavaro's opinion is that in addition to the Tilden-Vines singles performance, Tilden should also partner with a Shanghai Mecca, and Vines should partner with Canavaro himself or Mecca, for a doubles performance. Before the start, four Mecca players from this city will perform a doubles match as a prelude, for a total of three matches. Due to the time limit, each match will be three sets. This opinion has been sent to Mr. Tilden by express mail yesterday morning to seek his consent. As for the candidates for Mecca, it has not yet been decided, or Mecca will be selected by mutual recommendation. The performance time is expected to start between 2:00 PM and 2:30 PM. Tickets are divided into two types, 3 yuan and 5 yuan, and have been sent to the printer. They will be available for sale in the middle of next week. As for whether Mr. Tilden will be willing to attend another performance when he passes through Shanghai for the second time on his return trip, it is difficult to predict now. If the weather is too cold at that time, Mr. Tilden will not be willing to attend. If the weather is still as mild as last time, it will not be a problem, and I hope so very much. Currently, the bamboo canopy at Mr. Card's court at 153 Avenue Notre Dame has been removed, and a piece of vacant land from the Pu Yi Real Estate Company in front has been rented, and a Portuguese architect has been commissioned to design and build a grandstand with a capacity of 3,400 to 3,800 seats. The project is contracted by Gu Yongtai Bamboo Shop at the intersection of Xiaosha Ferry Road and Avenue Ivan, and construction started yesterday and is expected to be completed by the end of this month. Mr. Card also rented the grandstand seat boards from Shen Yuan the other day, and the deal is about to be concluded. The proposed performance program will be officially decided after Mr. Tilden agrees. Mr. Card himself has been unusually tired recently, and he may not be able to attend at that time. The tentative order is as follows:

(1) Doubles: Shanghai Mecca (candidates undecided)

(2) Singles: Tilden vs. Vines

(3) Doubles: Tilden and Shanghai Mecca vs. Vines and Canavaro or Mecca

Xiguang Cross-Country Team Hosts Shanghai-China Long-Distance Race; Registration Begins Tomorrow 100

The 4th Shanghai-China long-distance race, organized by the Xiguang Cross-Country Team and prepared by Wu Zhenqing and others, is generally ready. Registration will begin today, and the competition will be held on the morning of the 8th of next month. The association convened a preparatory meeting last night to discuss everything. The details are as follows:

Registration Begins Tomorrow

The 4th Shanghai-China long-distance race has been decided to start in front of the Minli Middle School on Zhonghua Road in Nanshi on the morning of the 8th of next month. Anyone over the age of 17 who is interested in long-distance running can apply to participate, regardless of qualifications. The registration office is at 25 Shanxi Road, and the registration period is limited to the end of this month.

Longhua Round-Trip Route

The Longhua round-trip route has been decided as follows: starting from the front gate of Minli Middle School, exiting Xiaoximen on Zhonghua Road, entering Daxing Street, Lujiabang, passing Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road, passing Shanghai Women's Middle School, Kaiming Middle School, turning right into Kangqu Road, passing Rihui Bureau Nanyang Middle School, Songhu Garrison Headquarters, and going straight to Chenjiawan, 1,000 meters south of the Longhua Pagoda, and then returning to the original address on Zhonghua Road. The entire course is 12 English miles, or approximately 20,000 meters. The team's highest record is held by Wang Zhenglin, the Chinese track and field athlete at this World Games, with a time of 1 minute, 03 minutes, and 6 seconds.

China Youth Association Initiates Indoor Games 101

To be held at 7:00 PM on the 24th

The Shanghai China Youth Association, in view of the fact that the weather has entered autumn and is getting cooler, the association has specially launched a one-week indoor sports event, hoping that all members will actively participate to achieve universal results. The rules are as follows:

Grouped Events (Time) October 24, 7:00 PM (extend by one or two nights if one night is not enough) (Location) Gym of the association, (Grouping) Divided into four groups: children (under 90 pounds), teenagers, adults, and men over 35, (Eligibility) All members of the association can participate, (Competition) Each group competes separately, (Registration) At the association on Sichuan Road, each event costs 5 cents, deadline is the evening of the 22nd

Competition Events (I) (Events) Ordinary events for each group (1) 60-yard potato race (2) 120-yard potato race, (3) 140-yard potato race, (4) 480-yard potato race, (5) Running high jump, (6) Standing long jump, (7) Putting the 12-pound shot put, (8) Pull-ups, (9) Rope climbing, (10) Sit-ups, (11) Push-ups, (12) Basketball shooting, (II) Six-event all-around (limited to teenagers and adults) (1) 60-yard potato race, (2) 160-yard potato race, (3) Running high jump, (4) Standing long jump, (5) Putting the 12-pound shot put, (6) Vaulting "Note" (1) Any event with less than four participants will be cancelled, (2) Each person is limited to joining one group of ordinary events, if more than one joins the six-event all-around, they must participate in all events, (3) Events cannot be changed after registration

Scoring Method (Scoring) Six-event scoring method, the top four in each event are scored 10, 6, 4, and 2 points. If two people have the same score, the one with the most first-place finishes in single events wins. If the tie cannot be broken with the most first-place finishes, then the one with the most second-place finishes wins, and so on. If the tie still cannot be broken, then one of the following two methods will be used as the final solution: (1) Draw lots, (2) Divide the prizes equally. (Awards) (1) Ordinary events for each group, four prizes for each event, one prize for less than five participants, no overall champion award, (2) Ten prizes for the six-event, four prizes for five or fewer participants, no prizes for each event, (3) The names of the winners of each event are engraved on the memorial tablet and will be admired forever, (Prizes) Solicited from major merchants, factories, and enthusiastic sports people, distributed by the association in advance, and displayed publicly for viewing.
