General Situation of Japanese Schools in Shanghai 108

— Special Dispatch from This Newspaper: Investigation by Hu Zuyin

(11) Women's Education

The purpose of Japanese women's education is to cultivate beautiful female virtues, with the aim of creating suitable good wives and wise mothers. The implementation is also progressing towards this monthly goal. Some courses in Japanese higher girls' schools, such as sewing, cooking, etiquette, tea ceremony, home decoration, and education, are prepared for female students to become good wives and wise mothers when they leave school in the future. The school currently has 13 graduating classes, with a total of 592 graduates. Among them, 181 are married, accounting for about one-third of all graduates.

The environment of the girls' school is very quiet and beautiful. The school building is surrounded by trees, and the open space is covered with green lawns. The special classrooms inside the school building are also very well equipped. The etiquette room for female students is divided into two types: one is decorated with several Japanese-style rooms, representing a typical Japanese family; the other is decorated with several foreign-style rooms, with a Western flavor. There are also two sewing rooms: one is a Japanese-style sewing room, where students learn to sew Japanese-style clothes; the other is a Western-style sewing room, where students learn to sew Western-style clothes. The cooking room is large, with multiple stoves, which can be used by students to practice Chinese, Japanese, and Western cooking. There is also a dyeing room, which can be used by students to practice dyeing clothes.

(12) Besides higher girls' schools, there are also Japanese vocational youth schools and Japanese commercial schools in Shanghai. The vocational youth school is a night school, with classes three hours every night. It is attached to the North Common Higher Elementary School and has classes in the school building. The school is of a remedial nature and only has three years of junior high school level. In terms of courses, in addition to Japanese language, ethics, and English, there is also a part of commercial courses, such as arithmetic, abacus, commercial knowledge, commercial geography, and bookkeeping. There are also four hours of Chinese per week, focusing on Shanghai dialect conversation and writing.

The commercial school is a formal commercial secondary school with a five-year curriculum and 34 hours of classes per week. The courses include ethics, Japanese language, mathematics, history, geography, natural science, physical education, drawing, commercial knowledge, and commercial practice. There is also a Chinese language course, taught for four hours per week per academic year, focusing on Mandarin conversation and writing. In the teaching of each subject, the focus is on cultivating commercial talents. For example: the national language, Chinese grammar, and composition focus on commercial application writing, and calligraphy focuses on commercial application fonts; numbers focus on commercial arithmetic and abacus; history and geography focus on world commercial history and commercial geography; drawing focuses on commercial advertising paintings. The commercial knowledge course focuses on bookkeeping, commercial law, statistics, and finance. Commercial practice is held in the fifth grade, focusing on import and export commercial practice and typing practice. Through this excellent training and practice, the commercial personnel cultivated by the school can meet the needs of society.

(End)

Finance Minister Kong Discusses Sino-British Credit Loan: A Common International Practice, Small in Amount, Not Worthy of Surprise 110

The New News Agency reports that Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and concurrently Minister of Finance, accompanied Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission from Nanjing to Shanghai by plane on the afternoon of Double Ten Day. After staying in Shanghai for one night, he took the Shanghai-Hangzhou express train to Hangzhou the next morning to attend the graduation ceremony of the Aviation Military Academy. He returned to Shanghai by car at about 10 PM the night before. Yesterday morning at 11:30 AM, he went to the Central Bank to review important official documents and met with Song Ziliang, Director of the Finance Department of Guangdong Province, Xu Kan, Vice Minister of Finance, Chen Xing, Vice President of the Central Bank, and others to inquire about everything. Subsequently, he met with reporters from various newspapers. Regarding the rumor that China and the United Kingdom were about to establish a credit loan, Kong did not deny it. However, the amount of the loan, the process of negotiation, and the content of the loan contract were not disclosed due to the early stage of negotiations. The main points of Kong's conversation stated that such loans are frequently negotiated between various countries and us, not just one country. Credit loans between countries are extremely common, and the amount is not large, so there is nothing to be surprised about. He hoped that the people of the country would not make neurotic speculations about such ordinary matters. Kong also spoke about the new gold standard agreement established by Britain, the United States, and France, saying that this kind of international monetary agreement is produced by stabilizing international exchange rates, which is a good phenomenon for international finance.

Baoshan Seawall Repaired After Breach 111

The Baoshan seawall, after being hit by autumn tides this year, was in a dangerous state. The breached areas included over 300 zhang of Bei Shi Dong, Liwai Yanchi, Bei Wang Miao, and Shi Qiang, as well as 42 zhang of the Chu Jing section. After the leaders of Tai, Jia, and Bao counties telegraphed the provincial government for emergency help, the Jiangsu Construction Department sent engineer Tu Jun to Baoshan to survey the damage and hire workers to rush repairs to the dangerous sections. The work has now been completed. After inspection and verification by Zhang Mingjing, the magistrate of Baoshan County, he immediately telegraphed the provincial department requesting funds to carry out permanent construction work.

Planning to Return to Guangdong Next Week

Song Ziliang, the Finance Commissioner and Director of Finance of Guangdong Province, visited Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi at the Central Bank again at about 11 AM yesterday to report in detail on the reorganization of finance in Guangdong Province and seek instructions on everything. The meeting lasted for about an hour. According to a reporter from the New News Agency, Song originally planned to return to Guangdong to take office soon, but due to overwork, he contracted liver disease and is currently staying in Shanghai for medical treatment. He is planning to leave Shanghai and return south next week.

New Life Movement Promotion Association Sends Letters Requesting Recommendations for Trainees 113

Quota of 170 Trainees

Training Session to Begin on the 1st of Next Month

The National News Agency reports that the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association, in order to actively promote the New Life Movement and cultivate talents for this purpose, has decided by the Executive Committee to hold a New Life Movement training session. Instructor Wu Tiecheng has been appointed as honorary president, Pan Gongzhan as president, and Jiang Hao as director of association affairs. The session is scheduled to officially begin on the 1st of next month at the Chamber of Commerce of Tianhougong Bridge, lasting for two months. Preparations are currently underway. As the time for the start of the session is approaching, the association has, based on the resolution, allocated quotas and sent letters to various institutions in the city requesting recommendations for trainees, so as to start the training session as scheduled. The allocated quotas and the official letters to the institutions are recorded below:

Allocated Quotas:

Party Affairs Organs: 20 trainees

Municipal Organs: 18 trainees

Social Education Organs: 8 trainees

School Organs: 70 trainees

Military and Police Organs: 10 trainees

Professional Organizations: 17 trainees

National Organs: 19 trainees

Other Organs: 2 trainees

Total: 170 trainees

Institutions and Organizations:

Municipal Party Headquarters, Security Corps Party Headquarters, Two Roads Party Headquarters, Seamen's Party Headquarters, Garrison Command, Security Corps Headquarters, Municipal Farmers' Association, Federation of Trade Unions, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Seamen's Union, Lawyers' Association, Accountants' Association, Physicians' Association, Pharmacists' Association, Traditional Chinese Medicine Association, Journalists' Association, Municipal Education Bureau, People's Welfare Committee, Children's Happiness Committee, 19 National Institutions, Municipal Government, Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, etc.

Original Text of the Circular:

"The New Life Movement is a crucial plan for national salvation. Since its establishment, this association has been actively promoting it in accordance with the essential points indicated by the president. However, this movement involves changing customs and reforming the old and establishing the new. If we only rely on the advocacy of a few people without enlightening others, the promotion will inevitably be hindered, and the results will be difficult to universalize. In view of this, this association has decided to organize the Shanghai New Life Movement Training Session for two months, starting from November 1st. Staff members will be designated by various institutions, schools, and organizations in this city and recommended to attend. This association will invite academic celebrities from the central and local levels who have a thorough understanding of the New Life Movement to serve as lecturers and impart various practical knowledge, so that the trainees will have a deeper understanding and a stronger belief in the New Life Movement in the future. They will become the center for promoting the New Life Movement in their original institutions, providing consultations for the supervisors, and promoting it locally, so that the results can be easily achieved. We have found that the quota for trainees in the training session is × people. We request your × to designate staff members from your institution and affiliated institutions (district party headquarters) (teams). We are enclosing the regulations and sending this letter for your reference. Please send the list of designated staff members to this association before the 22nd of this month for verification and to facilitate the process. Sincerely yours." There are also letters to the municipal government and the social affairs bureau instructing their affiliated institutions, which are mostly the same and are omitted here.

National Assembly Regional Representative Candidate Li Xiuling Declines Election 116

Lu Zhe Substitutes in the Office

The election office of the Shanghai National Assembly regional representatives has handled the nomination and announced the results. The results of the election were published in yesterday's newspapers. It is learned that the office has notified the 80 candidates elected the day before yesterday. However, Mr. Li Xiuling has replied, expressing his unwillingness to be elected. The office will, according to the law, substitute Lu Zhe, who received the next highest number of votes. The original letter from Li Xiuling is recorded below: "Dear Sirs, I have received your letter informing me that Xiuling has been elected as a candidate for regional representative of Shanghai. Since childhood, Xiuling has served in the military and dedicated himself to the country. In this time of national crisis, with foreign aggression pressing closer every day, the survival of the nation is in imminent danger, which is the time for soldiers to serve the country. As for the National Assembly, it is the foundation for nation-building and relies on wise men to offer grand plans and deliberations. Xiuling is a soldier and has never been involved in politics. Therefore, I sincerely decline and respectfully yield to the capable. I have decided not to be elected. I hope you will understand my humble intention. Sincerely, Li Xiuling, October 14th, addressed to the Shanghai Representative Election Office of the National Assembly."

Financial Sector Observation: UK Loan to China Problem, Believed to Benefit Both China and the UK, Total Loan Amount Approximately Five Million Pounds 117

The New News Agency reports that after the news of the impending establishment of a credit loan agreement between China and the United Kingdom was transmitted by the Free International Telegraph, the financial sector here paid close attention. According to the opinions of important figures in the banking sector, if this move is realized, not only will China's finance in the international market turn for the better, but also international trade will prosper as a result. Therefore, both China and the United Kingdom will jointly benefit from it. The negotiation of this priced loan agreement has a long history, dating back to when the British financial advisor Sir Frederick Leith-Ross came to China. After several discussions between the two parties, it is now about to mature. Although the total amount of the loan has not been determined, it is approximately 5 million pounds. Calculated at the current exchange rate, it is about 60 million yuan in national currency. However, the date of establishment of the loan agreement and the distribution of the amount of cash and goods in the total loan amount still need to be negotiated and decided by both parties.

Zhejiang Local Bank and Jiangxi Yumin Bank Facilitate Merchants and People 118

Mutual Exchange of Remittances and Substitute Exchange of Subsidiary Currency Notes, Sign Draft First, Then Formal Contract

The Zhejiang Local Bank and the Jiangxi Yumin Bank have agreed on measures for mutual exchange of subsidiary currency notes and mutual exchange of remittances in various parts of the two provinces. Xu Enpei, General Manager of the Zhejiang Local Bank, and Qian Chengxin, Deputy Manager of the Jiangxi Yumin Bank and Director of the Shanghai Office, signed the draft in Shanghai. The formal contract will be signed after approval by the head offices. The details are recorded as follows:

Substitute Exchange of Subsidiary Currency Notes

The Zhejiang Local Bank and the Jiangxi Yumin Bank are provincial banks in Zhejiang and Jiangxi provinces and have been approved to issue 1-, 2-, and 5-cent subsidiary currency notes. Since the opening of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, the two provincial banks have agreed on mutual exchange measures, stipulating that the branches of the two banks along and near the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, such as Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Jinhua, Lanxi, Longyou, Quzhou in Zhejiang, and Nanchang, Yushan, Hekou, Shangrao, and Guixi in Jiangxi, can mutually exchange them. Therefore, in the future, anyone holding subsidiary currency notes issued by the two provincial banks can apply for exchange at any time to the local branches of the two banks.

Mutual Exchange of Remittances

At the same time, in view of the increasing prosperity of commerce in the two provinces after the opening of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, the two provincial banks have agreed to mutually exchange remittances at the places where the two banks have established branches, in order to facilitate the transactions of merchants and people. It is also stipulated that the collection and transfer of funds between banks will be free of charge, and the fees charged to the outside world will be reduced as much as possible. The branches of the two banks are gradually spreading to various counties in the two provinces. Therefore, in the future, when the people of the two provinces need to exchange remittances for commercial purposes, they can apply for exchange at any time to the local branches of the two banks.

China Merchants and Six Other Companies Add Shallow Water Fees to Yangtze River Vessels 119

Effective from the 19th

After the China Merchants Bureau (state-owned), Sanbei Company (private), Ningshao Company, British Taikoo Company, Jardine Matheson Company, and Japanese Nisshin Company jointly cooperated in the apportionment of water transport expenses on the Shanghai-Hankou route, it has achieved good results. Now, as the autumn season approaches, the Yangtze River is shallow, navigation is slower, and more coal is needed. It is proposed to increase the shallow water fee to supplement funds. After the deliberation of the joint meeting of the six companies, the measures for increasing the collection of shallow water fees for goods are recorded in the announcement, which states: "Starting from October 19th, 1936, the shallow water fee for goods loaded from Hankou to Changsha and Xiangtan will be increased by 25%, and the shallow water fee for goods from Hankou to Changsha and Yichang will be increased by 15%. This is hereby announced."

Two Ships Run Aground Outside Haizhou Port 121

One Outside Haizhou Port, One at Chenjiagang Port

Hengshan

The Hengshan, owned by the Sanbei Company, weighs 1,922 tons and has a draft of 17 feet 6 inches. Recently, the ship was transporting salt in Haizhou. On Tuesday of this week (the 13th), at about 6 AM, the ship was loading a large amount of salt in Haizhou and heading for the Yangtze River. As soon as it left Haizhou Port, it encountered an extremely strong southwest wind, and the Hengshan ran aground in Haizhou Port. The captain measured the water and found that it was only 14 feet deep, but the Hengshan's draft was 17 feet 6 inches, causing the ship to sink deep into the beach and unable to move. The captain urgently reversed the engine to try to get out of the shallow water on its own, but all attempts failed. Until yesterday morning, after more than 20 hours, it was still difficult to escape. The captain telegraphed Shanghai for help. Upon receiving the news, the company urgently telegraphed the Fengpu ship, which is currently in Haizhou, ordering it to rush to rescue the Hengshan. At the same time, it telegraphed the captain of the Hengshan, ordering him to wait for the arrival of the Fengpu to tow it. The Fengpu has now arrived at the scene and is currently towing the ship.

Yunlong

The Yunlong, owned by the Shanghai Heng'an Chengji Shipping Company, weighs 1,770 tons and has a draft of 19 feet. The ship was recently sailing to the Yangtze River and Haizhou, specializing in transporting salt to various places upstream. Yesterday morning, Heng'an Company received an urgent telegram from the captain of the Yunlong, which stated that the ship had loaded all the salt in Haizhou and was sailing out of the port when it reached Chenjiagang Port. Due to the shallow water, the Yunlong was heavily loaded and had a deep draft, causing it to run aground. Even at high tide, it was unable to escape. After receiving the report, the Shanghai company telegraphed Haizhou to inquire about the current situation of the ship and devise a rescue plan. At the same time, the company also sent a letter to the China Ship Insurance Association for verification. The details of the grounding have been telegraphed to the captain for reporting. On one hand, it is considering sending a ship to tow it.

After the Annual Meeting of the Tea Industry Association Was Suspended, a Small Group Meeting Was Held Yesterday to Discuss Solutions. The Discussion Will Continue Today Due to the Absence of Wu Juenong. The Tea Industry Association Published Detailed Account of the Dispute. 125

Xinsheng News Agency reports that after the opening of the first annual meeting of the China Tea Industry Association, the general meeting was suspended the day before yesterday due to a dispute. After persuasion from party and government agencies, a small group meeting was held yesterday morning to discuss solutions. The discussion continued at 2 PM, but was postponed to today due to the temporary absence of Director Wu Juenong. The Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association released a detailed account of the events, which is recorded below:

Small Group Meeting

After a dispute arose over the issue of new members joining the Tea Industry Association, a small group meeting was held at 10 AM yesterday at the Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association in Gujia Lane after the persuasion of representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Party Department. Directors Wu Juenong and Zai Zhenhuan, Chairman of the Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association Ye Shichang, and tea merchant representatives from various places, including Chen Chucai, Yao Yiquan, and Zhang Jingyang, attended the meeting on time. First, the tea merchant representatives from various places expressed their opinions, requesting that new members and old members should be treated equally. The presidium of the general meeting accepted this in principle and scheduled a continuation of the meeting at the original location at 2 PM. However, due to the absence of Director and Presidium Member Wu Juenong, there were no results, and it was decided to hold another meeting today.

Published Account

Ye Shichang, Chairman of the Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association, released the following account yesterday: "(1) The reasons for the postponement of the annual meeting of the Tea Industry Association as reported in the evening newspapers of the 13th and the newspapers of the 14th, which stated that there was a conflict of opinions between political and business circles, are inconsistent with the facts. The tea merchants among the members have always made no expression to the government other than proposing suggestions to the government. When most of the members went to the social venue at the time, they saw two kinds of paper strips posted on the wall, one for attending members and one for non-voting members. They thought that the members attending the meeting had all received the meeting notice from the association, reported for registration, and had exercised their voting rights when selecting examiners on the 11th, so they naturally obtained membership qualifications. Suddenly, there was unequal treatment, and questions arose. The presidium was unable to explain for a while, so the party department instructor announced the postponement of the meeting. (2) On the afternoon of the 13th, Section Chief Wu Huanru of the Social Affairs Bureau expressed his opinions to the presidium and the member representatives, encouraging the members to unite in spirit, without the need to distinguish between new and old members, and advised them to hold a small group meeting. Once the opinions of all parties are consistent, then the general meeting will be continued to avoid disputes. (3) On the morning of the 14th, the presidium of the association convened tea merchant representatives at the Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association in Gujia Lane, Beijing Road, for a small group meeting. The opinions of the members who were designated as non-voting members were very simple, only requiring equal treatment across the board, without distinguishing between new and old members. There would be no problem. However, Mr. Wu Juenong believed that today's meeting should only increase the number of directors and not involve the issue of membership qualifications, but the majority believed that laws, articles of association, facts, and reason should all be considered and taken care of, and unity in spirit should be maintained. As a result, part of the presidium believed that members should no longer be distinguished between new and old and should be treated equally, while another part believed that there were still problems. The afternoon meeting had to be continued due to the absence of Wu Juenong. My opinion is that the Tea Industry Association is an organization in which people across the country jointly seek to improve and develop the tea industry. Members must all work together harmoniously. This kind of small misunderstanding will soon be eliminated. This association is working hard to mediate in order to achieve unity in spirit."

Reporting to the Government

The Yangzhuang Tea Industry Association sent Ye Shichang, Yu Xiji, and Zhu Yanqing to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau in the city center at 4 PM yesterday to report to Director Pan and Section Chief Wu on the details of the small group meeting, the absence of Wu Juenong, and the lack of results from the meeting. They returned at about 5 PM and reported on the trip to the Social Affairs Bureau to tea merchant representatives from various places and members of the association.

Henan Province Grain Export Measures 126

Purchasing or Transporting Requires a Purchase and Transport Certificate, Social Affairs Bureau Notifies Various Rice Industry Organizations

The Social Affairs Bureau issued instructions to trade associations of Miscellaneous Grains, Oil Cakes, Rice Industry, Rice Shops, and Rice Dealers, as well as the Rice Carriers Joint Association, stating that when purchasing goods from Henan, a purchase and transport certificate must be obtained. The Miscellaneous Grains Association should notify all members. The official document issued by the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau with the reference number 1739 stated that the Henan Provincial Government plans to formulate temporary measures for grain export and has forwarded the instructions to inform all businesses to comply with them. Copies of the Henan Provincial Temporary Measures for Grain Export and the purchase and transport certificate form are sent to the association for implementation and reference. The so-called grain mentioned above includes rice, wheat, soybeans, sesame, and other items. In the future, if businesses purchase the above-mentioned goods from Henan Province for shipment to Shanghai or other places, they should first report the name, tonnage, departure vehicle, and destination of the purchased goods to the Fourth Section of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to issue a grain purchase and transport certificate. If there are shipments in batches, they must also apply for the certificate in order, so as to purchase and transport. A copy of the Henan Provincial Temporary Measures for Grain Export and a copy of the grain purchase and transport certificate form are included.

Grain Export Measures

The text of the Henan Province Temporary Measures for Grain Export is as follows: Article 1: Flour mills or companies in and outside the province that purchase grain in this province must hold a purchase and transport certificate issued by the provincial and municipal governments where the factory or company is located. However, the certificate shall state: (1) the name and location of the factory or company; (2) the name of the purchaser and the place of purchase; (3) the type and quantity of grain purchased (in tons); (4) whether it is transported by land or water and to where. Article 2: Grain merchants in and outside the province who purchase grain in this province for export must hold a purchase and transport certificate issued by the provincial and municipal governments where the merchant is located. However, the certificate shall state: (1) the name and location of the merchant; (2) the name of the purchaser and the place of purchase; (3) the type and quantity of grain purchased (in tons); (4) whether it is transported by land or water and to where. Article 3: Those who purchase and transport grain in the province without leaving the province must hold a purchase and transport certificate issued by the county government where the merchant's store is located. Article 4: For those who purchase grain in large quantities in this province without a purchase and transport certificate, the county governments should prohibit them at any time, and the transportation agencies should refuse to transport them. Article 5: If the quantity of purchase and transport stated on the aforementioned purchase and transport certificate cannot be purchased or transported all at once, it can be purchased and transported in several times. Each time, the county government and transportation agency where it is located should indicate the quantity on the certificate, but the total quantity shall not exceed the original quantity. Article 6: When county governments issue purchase and transport certificates to grain merchants, they should verify that the grain merchants are purchasing and transporting grain to help the people's food supply before issuing them. However, no handling fee may be charged.

Grain Purchase and Transport Certificate

The original text of the grain purchase and transport certificate issued by the Social Affairs Bureau states: "The Provincial/Municipal/County Government of [Blank] issues the grain purchase and transport certificate. It is reported by [Blank] Company/Factory/Firm/Merchant that they intend to purchase [Blank] tons of [Blank] from [Blank] County, [Blank] Province, and transport them by [Blank] road/station/dock to [Blank] County, [Blank] Province. After verification by the Provincial/Municipal/County Government, it is confirmed to be true and there is no fraud. In accordance with Article [Blank] of the Henan Province Temporary Measures for Grain Export, a grain purchase and transport certificate is hereby issued as proof to [Blank] Company/Factory/Firm/Merchant for their use. Republic of China, [Blank] Month, [Blank] Day." This is a two-part form, with the lower part being the stub, with the same text, including "(In addition to issuing the purchase and transport certificate, this is kept for reference)."

Border-Crossing Road Section: Japanese Troops Conducted Drills Twice Yesterday; Discovery of Japanese Troops Parading on Avenue Edward VII; No Further Japanese Guards Patrolling Around Jiangwan Road 128

According to the New Voice News Agency, the situation in the Hongkou and Zhabei areas has been stable for several days. However, yesterday morning at about 9:30 AM, over a hundred Japanese soldiers gathered at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Dixiwei Road and conducted street fighting drills. They divided into two teams, passed through Yong'anfang and Fengleli to Doule'an Road, simulating an attack on the Japanese Marine Corps Headquarters on Jiangwan Road. The drills lasted for about half an hour. Again, at around 2:00 PM, over a hundred Japanese soldiers conducted field exercises near Hongkou Park, returning to camp at about 3:00 PM. It was found that both of yesterday's Japanese drills were conducted in the border-crossing road section. Also, at 3:50 PM yesterday afternoon, Japanese troops were again discovered parading on Avenue Edward VII, consisting of four trucks and five motorcycles, heading east and turning onto North Sichuan Road, returning to the Japanese Marine Corps Headquarters on Jiangwan Road. It was observed that they were returning from the western part of Shanghai. The Zhabei area was peaceful all day yesterday. No further Japanese patrols were seen around Jiangwan Road, and no further Japanese posts were found at Tongji Road, etc. According to the Central News Agency, a unit of Japanese soldiers is stationed at the Xuhui Dōbunshoin. Yesterday morning at about 10:30 AM, several junior officers, in a car, preceded by four motorcycles, followed by military trucks numbered 18, 21, 22, and 27, departed from the Dōbunshoin, turned onto Columbia Road, stopped at the intersection of Lujia Road, got out of the car for inspection, and after about half an hour, returned to the Dōbunshoin via the original route, taking Lujia Road and turning onto Haig Road.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notice: Term of Office for Branch Directors 129

Shall Not Exceed Two Years; Renewable Once

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued a notice to the Nanshi, Wusongjiang, and Pudong branch offices, stating: We are writing to inform you that the term of office for the directors of the Chamber's branch offices was previously stipulated by the Chamber in September of the 22nd year of the Republic. As the directors are appointed by the Standing Committee members of the Chamber, their term of office should be the same as that of the Standing Committee members. However, this regulation was not incorporated into the organizational charter of the branch offices after it was stipulated. It has now been resolved by the fifth executive committee meeting of the current session to add a clause to Article 2 of the Chamber's branch office organizational charter, stating that the term of office for a director who is a staff member of the Chamber shall be the term of their own position, and the term of office for a director who is not a staff member shall not exceed two years, and may be renewed only once. We are sending this notice to you for your information and compliance.

General Chamber of Commerce Telegram to Salt Affairs Administration: Please Release Wu Huinan 131

Wu Huinan, a supervisor of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, opened a Fengtai general store in Langxi County, Anhui Province. The area usually consumes Zhejiang salt. Last winter, due to a shortage of Zhejiang salt, he transported refined salt from Biqiao Town in the neighboring Yixian County for sale in the market. It was inspected, sealed, and ordered to be returned by Ling Xiaochao, the district chief of the sixth district of the Fifth Taxation District of Jiangsu. He requested permission to open the seal and return the salt to Biqiao. A small amount was kept for personal consumption. Then, Shao, the captain of the 58th team under the district, arrived in Langxi and ordered him to pay the price of the official salt. Wu Huinan complied and paid it. After appealing to the Chief Inspectorate, he was ordered to be handed over to the court for trial. While Wu Huinan was waiting for the summons for questioning, he was suddenly arrested at the Great China Hotel in the French Concession of the city on the 2nd of this month. The telegram from the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce to the Salt Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance is recorded as follows: Honorable Sir of the Salt Affairs Administration of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: It has been found that this association previously received a letter from Wu Huinan, a member of the Langxi Chamber of Commerce, regarding the case of transporting and selling refined salt across districts. This association telegraphed in the winter of this month to request that the illegal punishment by the tax police be stopped. Recently, a letter from Wu Huinan's family stated that Wu Huinan was falsely accused of being a smuggler by Shao, the captain of the 98th team of the sixth district of the Fifth Taxation District of Jiangsu, and was arrested on the 2nd of this month and detained at the Shanghai Local Court for more than ten days. Wu Huinan is over sixty years old, old and sick. This torture has caused a threat to his life. They requested that it be forwarded to the court for redress. Based on this, it was found that the refined salt had already paid national taxes and was not smuggled salt. The problem only arose due to the wrong district. Moreover, the salt was ordered to be returned, and the salt price had already been paid. The matter was also reported to the Salt Affairs Chief Inspectorate, and an instruction was issued to transfer it to the local court for trial. He should have waited for the court to summon him for questioning according to the law. Now, the court has not yet issued a summons, but the captain has falsely accused him of being a smuggler and has arbitrarily arrested and detained him. The people have lost the protection of the law. Correspondingly, we are telegraphing again to your administration for review, immediately requesting that you issue a telegram order to release Wu Huinan and allow him to wait for the local court to summon him for questioning in order to clarify the truth and uphold the law. This is our earnest hope. National Federation of Chambers of Commerce.

Political Prisoner Education Association: Second Phase of Work Underway 133

Currently Surveying the Number of Inmates in Various Prisons

The Municipal Party Headquarters of this city, in order to correct the thinking of political prisoners in various district prisons and instill the Three Principles of the People to promote genuine reflection, has established the Shanghai Municipal Political Prisoner Education Committee. Committee members have been selected to go to various prisons in phases to provide education. The first phase, involving 103 political prisoners, began on July 1 and ended on September 30. After review by the committee, those with good conduct, level of education, and academic qualifications will be identified as outstanding and referred to the court for transfer to a reformatory, so that they can repent and reform, and regain their freedom. The committee believes that educating political prisoners is of great significance to national thought and social relations. Therefore, the second phase of education work is being carried out. A survey form for the number of political prisoners in various prisons has been prepared and is being conducted. As soon as the survey is completed, education will be organized and implemented, scheduled to begin on November 1.

Municipal Council Implements Austerity Measures: Resolves to Abolish Intelligence Office 137

The Municipal Council held a regular meeting yesterday (the 14th) and proposed austerity measures. In addition to deciding to suspend the Vehicle Season Pass Association, it also resolved to abolish the Intelligence Office at the end of this year. The Municipal Council's Intelligence Office was established in 1931 and has been in existence for more than five years. Its performance has been highly praised by the Board of Directors. Unfortunately, due to severe financial difficulties, it has to be abolished. It is said that after the Intelligence Office is abolished, all news and intelligence will continue to be provided to the press, but the work will be transferred to the Chief Secretary's Office, with one assistant in the Chief Secretary's Office in charge. Newspaper reporters can inquire about all news about the Municipal Council at any time. All press releases will also be published by the Intelligence Assistant under the supervision of the Chief Secretary. The Director-General and the Chief Secretary of the Municipal Council will also schedule dates to meet with newspaper reporters to release all important news. It is also reported that after the Intelligence Office is abolished, it can save about 46,000 yuan per year.

Yu Siyong and Others Come to Shanghai to Discuss: Participation in Nanjing National Products Exhibition 138

National Products Manufacturers Association: Scheduled to Host a Banquet Tonight

The Nanjing National Products Exhibition Hall's Autumn National Products Exhibition this year is scheduled to open on the 10th of next month. Yu Siyong, the director of the hall, and others have come to Shanghai to discuss the participation of Shanghai factories. The Shanghai Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association is scheduled to host a banquet tonight and discuss the participation procedures. The details are recorded as follows:

Coming to Shanghai for Discussions

In order to promote domestic products and expand sales, the Nanjing National Products Exhibition Hall holds national products exhibitions in the spring and autumn every year. This year's autumn national products exhibition is scheduled to open on November 10 and will include a temporary market, which will be on a very large scale. Shanghai manufacturers are welcome to participate. The Nanjing National Products Exhibition Hall has contacted the Shanghai Chinese National Products Manufacturers Association by letter and telegram several times. As the opening date is approaching and many matters need to be decided, the director of the hall, Yu Siyong, and the chief of the General Affairs Section, Wang Jieping, have specially come to Shanghai to discuss everything in person. They arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday morning. Yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, accompanied by Zhu Boyuan of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, they visited the National Products Exhibition on Jing'an Temple Road and greatly praised the arrangements of the various factories. Lin Kanghou, chairman of the Shanghai Manufacturers Association, and executives Xu Xiaochu, Chen Youyun, Le Fucheng, and Liu Zhongying are also scheduled to host a banquet at Zhimeilou on Simalu tonight, during which the participation procedures will be discussed.

Participation Methods

Methods for the Temporary Market of the 25th Autumn National Products Exhibition of the Nanjing National Products Exhibition Hall: (1) In order to promote domestic products and expand sales, this hall will gather products from manufacturers from various places during the exhibition period to set up a temporary market to promote publicity and facilitate selection. (2) The business period of the temporary market is temporarily set at 20 days, opening and closing at the same time as the exhibition. (3) Manufacturers who join the temporary market must fill out a letter of intent, guaranteeing that they can abide by all the regulations of this association. (4) Manufacturers who join the temporary market are limited to the original products of the factory and may not sell products from other companies. Otherwise, once found, they may be temporarily suspended from business. However, if the manager has a certificate from the original factory and is verified by this association to be true, they may participate in the business in the name of the original manufacturer, but only one manager is allowed. (5) The sales booth for each manufacturer will be provided by this association, and a rent of 30 yuan will be charged for each booth. It shall not be changed for any reason during the exhibition period. (6) Each manufacturer will be provided with two lanterns by the hall, each limited to 25 watts, free of charge. However, if larger light bulbs are added or additional lamp holders are installed, they must first be reported to and approved by the association and pay the fee in advance according to the prescribed price. The lights shall be turned on and off according to the specified time, and manufacturers shall not arbitrarily request changes. The closing time will be temporarily determined by the association. (7) The selling time of this association is 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM every day, and a bell will be rung as a signal. (8) Manufacturers who join the temporary market to sell products must send their own personnel to manage and keep them. This association is not responsible for any accidental losses. (9) Manufacturers must submit the total daily sales income to this association truthfully for statistics. The format of the form will be determined separately. (10) Manufacturers must report any foreign affairs on business matters to this association for verification. (11) Manufacturers shall compensate at the price for any damage to the equipment and sundries of this association. (12) After the price of the manufacturer's sales products is marked, it shall not be arbitrarily raised or lowered in order to show fairness. The daily exchange rate will be indicated by this association. If the above regulations are violated and found by this association, it will be handled in accordance with the market rules of this hall. (13) Those who serve in the association will be given a badge to wear for identification. (14) If manufacturers wish to insure their products, they must report to this association before the meeting. (15) Matters such as fire protection, sanitation, and inspection shall be handled by this association. (16) If there are any matters not specified in these rules, the provisions of the market operating rules of this hall shall apply. (17) If there are any matters not covered in these measures, this association may amend them at any time. (18) These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. Note: The opening date of this association is November 10.

Carriage Pullers Mutual Aid Association Board of Directors Resolves to Reorganize; New Licenses for Carriage Pullers to Be Issued Starting January Next Year; More Than 2,700 New Cars Currently in the City 140

Regarding the reorganization of the board of directors of the Carriage Pullers Mutual Aid Association, the Municipal Council's Special Committee on Carriage Pullers recently convened a meeting on Monday this week (the 12th) to discuss it. According to the opinions of the Chinese members, there is no need for representatives of car dealers and carriage pullers on the board of directors, and the Mutual Aid Association fees do not need to be collected from carriage pullers by car dealers in the future. They can be supplemented by increasing the license fee. In this way, these funds will belong to the income of the Municipal Council, and the Municipal Council can consider dividing these funds as the Municipal Council's donation to the Mutual Aid Association. As for the organization of the Custodial Committee, it may remain the same, that is, one person will be appointed by the Municipal Council's Board of Directors, and one person each will be recommended by the Chinese Ratepayers Association and the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the three will jointly organize it. However, the board of directors will inevitably have to be reorganized, and the existing 12 members can be reduced to nine, with three members each recommended by the Municipal Council, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Chinese Ratepayers Association, and car dealers and carriage pullers may not be appointed as directors. The above suggestions have been approved by the Special Committee on Carriage Pullers and submitted to the Board of Directors. At the same time, it was solemnly stated that the donations that the Municipal Council intends to give to the Mutual Aid Association may be stopped by the Municipal Council at any time depending on the circumstances, and the representatives of the Municipal Council on the board of directors may not be Municipal Council staff. The above suggestions were unanimously approved at the regular meeting of the Municipal Council yesterday (the 14th).

In addition, regarding the issuance of new licenses to public carriage pullers, it has now been decided to start on January 4 next year and end on February 25. Within this prescribed period, each person will pay 20 cents per license, which will be deducted from the Municipal Council's donation to the Mutual Aid Association. After the deadline, the fee will be 50 cents. From March 1, carriage pullers who do not wear the appropriate armband will not be allowed to engage in carriage pulling. According to the survey, as of October 12, there were 2,727 new-style carriages in the Shanghai International Settlement.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asks Jiangsu Provincial Government: Strictly Arrest Pirates and Robbers of Magnetic Vessels 141

Robbed Twice in Recent Months; Please Order Strict Arrests to Ensure the Safety of Transport Merchants

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting the strict arrest of bandits and robbers to ensure the safety of merchants. The original telegram is recorded as follows: Jianzhen Jiangsu Provincial Government: It was reported on the 13th of this month that the Magnetic Industry Association stated in a letter that, according to reports from its members, the Chen Hongfa sailboat hired from Jingdezhen, Jiangxi to transport porcelain to Shanghai was traveling to Xingang, Rucao County, sixty miles above Tongzhou, when, due to wind resistance, it anchored in the harbor as usual. Unexpectedly, at about 9:00 PM on September 12, it was suddenly robbed by more than a dozen bandits with weapons, and 16 pieces of porcelain were lost. The boatman reported it to the local public security bureau, which sent personnel to investigate on file, etc. It has been found that the members of the association purchase goods in Jingdezhen, Jiangxi, and transport them to Shanghai for sale, which is purely a transport business. The cost of traveling on the Yangtze River is no less than several million yuan this year, and on May 29 this year, the Wang Caihua sailboat transporting porcelain was also robbed of 79 pieces of porcelain by bandits in Xiaoligang, Nantong County, more than ten miles above Tongzhou. The local water public security bureau and the Nantong County District Office were requested by the association to strictly investigate the case, but after several months, it was impossible to capture them. It seems that the bandits are rampant and arbitrarily robbing, which not only disturbs merchants and civilians, but also affects local security, which is particularly important. This is a special letter to your association, asking you to forward it to the relevant competent authorities and order them to strictly arrest the case and punish them according to the law, so as to pacify the bandits and facilitate the public, etc. The association has found that there have been frequent cases of robbery of merchant ships in Tongru County in recent years. Although they have been reported and arrested, few cases have been solved, which makes the navigation of merchant goods dangerous. Judging from the cases reported by various industries, first, the pig boats of the fresh pig industry were robbed many times, and now the porcelain boats have been robbed twice in recent months. The robbery case of May 29 has been more than four months, and there is still no news of the arrest. It seems that the bandits are rampant, the water police are slack, and how can merchants and travelers rest easy? It is reasonable to report the situation to your government for review, please strictly order your subordinates to investigate and arrest the cases separately, in order to solve the entire case and recover the stolen goods, so that transport merchants will not suffer losses, and it is hoped that it will be achieved. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Shangbao Hotel: Cracking Down on Tattoo Gang 142

Li Xingcai and Wang Tianba; Five People Claim to Be Tattoo Artists

The Shangbao Hotel at the intersection of Datong Road and Zhongxing Road, Zhabei, to the west of the Daxing Vegetable Market, at around 1:00 AM yesterday morning, just after the amusement park on the upper floor of the vegetable market dispersed, six tourists wearing blue cloth shirts and trousers opened room No. 5 in the hotel. At that time, Xie Xiong, the patrolling police chief of the Xinzha Public Security Bureau, and police officers Chi Baoren and others passed by and found that none of the tourists were registered in the tourist circulation book and that their behavior was suspicious, so they immediately entered the room for questioning. According to them, one of the six people, Li Xingcai (nicknamed Little Ningbo), was good at drawing flowers on people's arms (that is, the so-called tattoo gang), and they all went to ask him to tattoo them, and there was nothing else going on. A search of the room did not find any contraband. Police Chief Xie was concerned that in such a troubled place, these people might be holding secret meetings to plot wrongdoing, so they were all taken to the bureau. After questioning by the bureau staff, Li Xingcai claimed to be 20 years old, from Ningbo, living on Chang'an Road, Hanzhong Road, but did not know the house number, and admitted to tattooing people without concealment. He then took out a pencil and drew a Huang Tianshuang on the spot as proof. The other five people were named Ge Rucheng, 21 years old, from Funing, living in a thatched shed at the end of Datong Road; Yu Gaosheng, 28 years old, from Yancheng, also living in a thatched shed on Datong Road; Sun Rujiang, 28 years old, from Funing, living at No. 1 Hutai Road; Li Chuntao, 25 years old, from Yancheng, living in a thatched shed on Hutai Road; and Tang Guicai, 24 years old, from Yancheng, living in a thatched shed at the end of Zhijiang Temple Road, making a living by pulling rickshaws. The five people confessed that they had nothing to do after the theater ended, so they went to the hotel to play and asked Little Ningbo to tattoo them. After the interrogating officer verified the confessions, because Li Xingcai and the other six people were hiding in the hotel, fearing that they were not good people, in addition to instructing the original police chief to investigate and reply in detail and wait for verification and handling, Little Ningbo and the other six people were sent to the detective team for investigation.

Xiao Qingfu Injured by a Car 146

Qingjiang native, Qingfu, 45 years old, around 10 PM the night before last, was walking on Wanzhu Street next to the Wanzhu School on Luxiangyuan Road in Shanghai, when he was hit and run over in the waist and ribs by a car with the Shanghai license plate number 4322. The Murderer of Zhang Longhai, Yang Chunyi, is Apprehended; Arrested in Bengbu and Escorted to Shanghai; Admitted to the Murder During Interrogation 147

—Shanghai Postal Workers' Union Attaches Great Importance to This Case—

Zhang Longhai, a mailman from the Shanghai Central Post Office, was at his residence at 131 Jiangwan Hetan West Road around 8 PM on July 15th of this year when Yang Chunyi, who was supposedly a policeman in the city, broke in through the front door and shot Zhang several times in the chest with a handgun. The bullets hit vital organs, and he died immediately. At the same time, Zhang Longhai's concubine, Shen Cuie, was also shot and killed. Shen Cuie's younger sister, Shen Sifang, was also shot once, but fortunately, it was not fatal. The murderer, Yang Chun, fled the scene immediately. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union repeatedly sent letters to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, strictly ordering the arrest of the murderer, but no arrests were made. On the 7th of last month, the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union received a report from Shen Sifang, the younger sister of Zhang Longhai's concubine Shen Cuie, stating that Yang Chunyi, the murderer of Zhang Longhai, had recently sent a letter from Bengbu (attached below), where he is now employed, requesting that he be arrested quickly to uphold the law. The union immediately sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, requesting them to order detectives to go and arrest him at the address provided. The bureau then dispatched personnel to cooperate with the Bengbu Public Security Bureau to arrest him. The murderer was then apprehended and has now been escorted to Shanghai and transferred to the local court for interrogation. He was interrogated once the day before yesterday (the 12th) and directly admitted to the murder. A second interrogation is scheduled for tomorrow (the 16th), and a sentence will be announced at a set date. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union attaches great importance to this case. The details of the incident and the confession of the offender Yang are described below:

Yang's Letter to Shen Sifang

Respectful greetings to Uncle and Aunt Si Lin,

I hope you are well. I left Shanjiangwan on the fifteenth of last month and have not been able to report back since. I stayed in Nanjing for many days and was ill with a venereal disease. I could not find work and have now returned to Bengbu. I have been living on Er Ma Road for over a month and have fully recovered. I have now joined the Bureau of Finance with a salary of twenty yuan per month. I am short of clothes and bedding. After I have purchased them, I will send the remaining money home for Xiaogou, Yuying, and Yuemei to use. Do not be too sad about the Jiangwan incident. People cannot be brought back to life. It was their fate. I hope Sifang (Xiaomei) studies hard and works hard at school. Do not listen to outside gossip. What happened before was my fault. Please do not always remember it. Please give my regards to Lu Gaofa and Gao Jinhu's mother, the rice shop owner's wife, and Boss Qinchang. I will write again next time. Sincerely. Also, please ask Gu Meisheng to pay back the twenty yuan he borrowed, and Wei Shouye (from the police station in the 2nd precinct, Yongxing Road, 5th district) to return the fourteen yuan he owes. If you get it back, you can use it to buy tinfoil for (Longhai and Cuie). Sincerely. I wish you both good health.

From your nephew, Yang Chunyi.

Yang Chunyi's Written Confession

Yang Chunyi, 32 years old, from Nan Suizhou, Anhui Province, formerly served as a policeman in the North Railway Station Branch in Shanghai for about nine years. After completing his duties, he met a woman named Shen Cuie. The woman had a relationship with a postman after a long period of time. The policeman used up all the money he had. He then heard that she had a relationship with a man named Xiaobao at 131 Jiangwan Hetan Road. They quarreled many times. Her younger sister tried to persuade them, but then she had a relationship with the postman Zhang Longhai. The policeman was heartbroken and attempted suicide unsuccessfully. Later, his mother often went to the hospital, bringing Cuie to visit him. They reconciled. After the policeman was discharged from the hospital, he was transferred from the North Railway Station Branch to the First Squadron of the Public Security Bureau. His mother and Cuie often went to the bureau, saying how good he was. The policeman continued to visit them, often going to Jiangwan and his mother-in-law's house. His mother-in-law often made trouble at home because of money. The policeman handed over the accounts to his mother-in-law to manage. Because of training, he could not visit often. Shen Sifang, also known as Xiaomei, also had a relationship with Zhang Longhai. The policeman then attempted suicide by cutting himself. He attempted suicide at Lu Senji Timber Shop at 165 Zhonghua Xin Road. At the same time, Lu Gaofa reported to Police Chief Liu Huanlin. He called the Public Security Bureau and the Fire Brigade ambulance. He was sent to Shanghai Public Hospital for treatment. Around 2:40 PM on September 22nd of the 20th year, he reconciled with his family. He then went to the Public Security Bureau to collect his belongings. He returned to the team at four or five o'clock. Because all the policeman's clothes were stored at his mother-in-law's house, she took care of everything. Because Xiaomei did not come back for dinner, the policeman asked his mother-in-law why she did not come. She said she went to Jiangwan to make a living for a few days. The policeman was resentful. He took his own handgun to Jiangwan at 6:10 PM on July 15th of this year. He went to her house at 131 Hetan Road and fired three shots at the three people. He then fled. He did not know if they were dead or alive. The policeman then took a small path south of the railway and fled to a small inn on Baoxing Road, North Sichuan Road. He then wrote a letter to the First Squadron of the Public Security Bureau. At night, the policeman took the gun east on North Sichuan Road and handed it over to the patrol in front of the road, placing it on the ground. The policeman urinated and looked towards her house. The policeman went to the Tilanqiao Wharf. After arriving in Nanjing, he failed to find a job. He then went to the recruitment office of the 56th Division in Bengbu and became a messenger.

Yang Chunyi's personal confession, the 15th day

The Court Scheduled Another Hearing for Tomorrow

The suspect Yang was escorted from Bengbu to Shanghai and immediately transferred to the Nanshi Local Court for interrogation. During the first interrogation the day before yesterday (the 12th), the suspect directly admitted to the murder, providing the same confession as before. The court has now scheduled another interrogation for tomorrow (the 16th) and will announce a sentence at a fixed date. The local Postal Workers' Union attaches great importance to this case.

Blood Soul Assassination Squad Throws Bomb; Victim Testifies in Court; Defendants Admit Separately; Case Concluded, Sentence Announced on the 21st 148

Liu Hantao, Chuan Chaobai, Yin Jiafu, Wang Dongcai, Guan Yaoting, and five other members of the Blood Soul Assassination Squad were arrested by the Public Concession police in August for throwing bombs at various shops in the Public Concession to warn against the sale of inferior goods. They were prosecuted by the First Special District Court and sentenced to imprisonment. The French police then found that Liu and others had also committed similar crimes in the French Concession. The First Special Court transferred Liu and others to the case and sent them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. It was later found that the defendants had thrown bombs at four locations: Xie Da Xiang Foreign Goods Store on Xiaodongmen Main Street, Yuanhe Sugar Store on Xinkaihe Road in the Republic, Rixin Sheng Foreign Goods Store on Fada Road, and the home of wealthy merchant Bei Runsheng on Beile Road. The French Concession police filed a public prosecution with the Second Special Court in accordance with Articles 151, 154, and 181 of the Criminal Code for disrupting order and endangering public safety. The defendants hired lawyers Wu Peng and Fan Gang for defense. Judge Chen Ying repeatedly held hearings to investigate the case. Because the witnesses were not all present, the hearing was adjourned to another date for further examination. All the details were reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Chen continued the trial in the First Criminal Court. The witness Bei Runsheng testified that his home was bombed twice, on November 29th, 1933, and January 8th, 1934, at around 6 or 7 PM. The first time the glass windows were destroyed, and the second time the bomb did not explode in the garden. Both times, the police were notified. Before the incident, he received an anonymous letter saying that there was something to be sent to him. The representative of Yuanhe Sugar Store, Mr. He, said that a bomb was thrown on the drying platform sometime in February of the 20th year, but he could not remember the exact date. The bomb damaged the Stirling lock, and the shell was taken away after reporting to the police. The representative of Xie Da Xiang said that on November 18th, 1935, at 4 PM, there was a sudden explosion under the shop window, damaging the glass and the foreign cloth. The defendants admitted to the above-mentioned facts. The court believed that the facts of the case were clear and ordered the opening of the debate. Police lawyer Fei Xizhen argued that the police charged defendants 1, 3, 4, 5 with articles 151, 154, and 181 of the Criminal Code, and the second defendant with articles 151 and 154 of the Criminal Code. Four plaintiffs testified in court and the defendants admitted to throwing bombs separately. The content of their crimes was a warning, but not an act of fraud. The defense lawyer then made a defense for the defendants. The court announced the conclusion of the case and set the date for sentencing on the morning of the 20th. The defendants were returned to custody.

Zhang Xian's Posthumous Works Exhibition Opens Yesterday 151

The exhibition of the late painter Mr. Zhang Xian's posthumous works opened yesterday on the fourth floor of the Great New World Department Store. More than 100 pieces of his posthumous works were displayed, mostly traditional Chinese paintings and line drawings of figures, dynamic and evocative, with an elusive sense of strength, uniquely pioneering a new era in the national art scene. The audience was quite enthusiastic. At 5 PM, the opening ceremony was held. Over 200 people attended, including Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, Du Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Liu Haisu, President of the Shanghai Art College, and famous painters Wang Jiyuan and Pan Liangyu. His impoverished widow and orphans were especially pitiful. The Shanghai Municipal Council Decides to Discontinue the Wheelbarrow Committee 152

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Rickshaw Committee, also known as the Wheelbarrow Committee, was established in May 1934. For more than two years, it has spared no effort in improving the rickshaw affairs in the Public Concession and has achieved remarkable results. It is reported that at the regular meeting of the Board of Directors of the Shanghai Municipal Council yesterday (October 14), the recommendations of the Special Rickshaw Committee were adopted, and it was decided that the Wheelbarrow Committee would be discontinued at the end of this year. All rickshaw affairs will be transferred to the Police Department thereafter. According to the report submitted by the Special Committee, since the establishment of the Wheelbarrow Committee, its tasks have now been completed, such as the registration and licensing of rickshaw pullers, which have now been completed, and the number of new-style vehicles on the market has now reached 3,000. The rickshaw rent has also been reduced twice. In the future, the Police Department can handle rickshaw affairs as a normal part of its duties. In addition, at the beginning of the establishment of the Wheelbarrow Committee, the term of office was originally set for half a year. When the half-year term expired, it was felt necessary to extend it. Now that the work has been completed, the transfer to the police authorities for continued operation will save a huge amount of money for the Municipal Council's finances each year. There are still two and a half months before the end of the year, which is more than enough to handle the transfer. The continued operation by the police after that will not be inferior to the previous operation.

Female Worker Enamored of Becoming a Dancer, Father Locks Her Feet; Although Parent Cannot Violate the Law; Court Finds and Sentences to a Fine 153

Sun Lindi, a Ningbo woman (18 years old), lives at No. 8 Helin Lane, Yulin Road. She used to be a female worker in the tin packing section of the Huacheng Cigarette Factory on Huishan Road. Recently, she was lured by her girlfriends to change her career and learn to dance at the Xu Xiang Dance Hall on Fuzhou Road. Her father, Sun Xiaohua, was very unhappy about this and beat her. Lindi was enamored of the life of a dancer and often sneaked out. Her father could not stop her. At 9 AM on the morning of the 12th of this month, he bought an iron chain and two small locks from a hardware store and locked his daughter's feet to the bed, preventing her from stepping out. Until noon the day before yesterday, Detective Xie Wanfang and Detective Liu Zhisheng of the Chinese Detective Team discovered this, rushed to the address, and saw the woman groaning on the bed calling for help. Sun Xiaohua happened to be out shopping and had taken the key with him. He did not return until after 2 PM. After he was asked to open the lock, he was arrested along with the lock and chain and taken to the Yulin Road Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Municipal Council lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated the case and filed a public prosecution for the crime of obstructing freedom under Article 301, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, and stated that although the defendant was the woman's parent, he could not use this illegal means. He requested an investigation. Detective Xie then reported the course of events and presented the evidence. The woman, Lin Di, explained the past. The defendant was questioned and stated that he did not want his daughter to be a dancer and wanted her to work in the cigarette factory. Judge Xiao Xiefen sentenced Sun Xiaohua to a fine of 30 yuan. If he could not pay the fine, he would be sentenced to labor service, with 2 yuan equaling one day. The sentence was suspended for two years. The evidence was confiscated.

Ge Guanfu, a typesetter for this newspaper from Suzhou, lived at No. 11 Sanduo Lane, Daji Road, Nanshi. Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia and Inspector Xuan Zhiming were commissioned to conduct the inspection. They found that the deceased Ge Guanfu, 35 years old, from Suzhou, was wearing a white cloth short shirt and pants, white socks, and cloth shoes. His head was near the side of the bed, and his body was lying horizontally on the ground. His neck had been pierced, forming a hole about one inch deep and wide and about three inches long, shaped like it had been stabbed with a sharp knife. The trachea had been severed, confirming that he died from the injury before his death. They also inspected the miscellaneous items in the room, which were in a messy state, leaving a kitchen knife. They then questioned the corpse's mother. The corpse's mother was Ge's stepmother, who stated that her daughter-in-law was unusually fierce. Her husband's death and her escape clearly indicated conspiracy and requested investigation and arrest for prosecution. It was also learned that Ge was a member of the Municipal Newspaper Industry Workers' Union. Maoli Shipping Bureau Purchases New Fudong Ship 155

Renamed Maoli No. 2, Resuming the Shanghai-Taizhou Route

Xin Sheng Agency reports that since the sinking of the New Maoli ship on its maiden voyage, the Maoli Shipping Bureau has temporarily abandoned the Shanghai-Taizhou route and has been running the old Maoli ship exclusively on the Beisha route. The bureau's manager, Hong Baoshun, has now purchased the former Fudong ship from the Funing Shipping Company for a price of 80,000 yuan. The ship has a gross tonnage of 1,411 tons and a net tonnage of 823 tons, built in 1912. The transaction has been completed, and the ship is being repaired at the Jiangnan Shipyard of the Naval Department. It has also been registered and transferred to the Shanghai Shipping Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and renamed Maoli No. 2. Once the repairs are completed, the original Shanghai-Taizhou route will be resumed.

Hankou Road One-Way Traffic to be Abolished 156

Date to be Announced After Board of Directors Decides

Since the implementation of one-way traffic on Hankou Road, merchants in the area have repeatedly suggested to the Municipal Council that it be abolished, as it affects their business. This matter has been brewing for a long time. On the 6th of this month, the Shanghai Municipal Council's Security Committee re-discussed the matter, expressing sympathy for the obstruction of commerce. According to the opinion of the Police Chief, it seems that the abolition of one-way traffic will not cause major obstacles to vehicle traffic. After the abolition of one-way traffic on Hankou Road, vehicles will be diverted to Edward Road and Fuzhou Road, and the congestion on Nanjing Road will not increase excessively. Therefore, the Security Committee resolved to request the Board of Directors to approve the abolition of the current one-way traffic on Hankou Road. Japanese Porcelain Imported to Shanghai in Nine Months Reaches 900,000 157

Sells Well in Various Places, But the Quality is Very Poor

Shenshi Agency reports that Chinese porcelain is famous worldwide, with annual exports reaching 1 million yuan, sold to England, America, the Philippines, Siam, India, and other places. In recent years, India, Siam, Southeast Asia, and other places have been affected by the competition of Japanese porcelain, and the export of Chinese porcelain has been greatly impacted. As the special forces of Japan extend into China, Japanese porcelain goods flow into China continuously. Since the "September 18th" Incident in the three northeastern provinces, porcelain from Jiangxi and other places has been unable to be exported beyond the customs. The porcelain market in North China this year is flooded with smuggled goods. As for the import of Japanese porcelain to Shanghai this year, it has reached about 900,000 yuan in nine months. The exports and imports of Chinese porcelain do not offset each other, and there is a trade deficit. It is reported that the current Japanese porcelain imports are mainly vegetable bowls, bowls, teacups, and other items, which sell well in Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Suzhou, Wuhan, and other places. Their appearance is full of Japanese artistic colors, but the quality is very poor. They are not as durable as Chinese porcelain and break easily. However, Chinese people do not know the quality and blindly buy Japanese goods, resulting in significant losses.

Foreign Ship Collides with Barge, Kerosene Sinks into the Huangpu River 158

Kerosene Ship Split in Two, Wang Abing Negotiating

Yesterday morning at 6:50, the foreign ship Roanoke entered the port. At about 8 AM, it sailed to the Huangpu River near the Longmao Wharf in Lujiazui. At that time, a kiln goods ship with the number 27818, fully loaded with tiles and kiln goods, was coming from south to north. Behind it was a barge with the number 34065, carrying 1,170 cans of kerosene, continuing to follow. When the foreign ship sailed to the front of Longmao Wharf, the bow of the ship violently collided with the middle cabin of the kerosene barge, splitting it in two. The ship immediately sank, and all 1,170 cans of kerosene also sank into the Huangpu River. The boatmen who fell into the water were rescued by nearby sampans. About 300 cans of oil that were floating on the river were salvaged. After the accident, the ship continued to move forward. Barge boss Wang Abing and Ye Jiali have reported to the Jianghai Customs Water Police Station. The broken ship has been towed to the Jiangbian River in Pudong for beaching. Negotiations are underway.

Royal Asiatic Society Lecture Today 159

The Royal Asiatic Society at 20 Museum Road is scheduled to hold the opening lecture of the season today at 5:30 PM. The speaker is the President of the Society, Mr. Su Wenpei, who will speak on "Animals in Chinese Art." Mr. Su has a well-cultivated background in art and is also a naturalist. He is known for his research on Chinese flora and fauna. Mr. Su specializes in art and natural history. He is particularly interested in identifying the types of birds, mammals, reptiles, aquatic animals, and insects depicted by Chinese artists and craftsmen, and in researching the reasons for their choice of materials or specimens, and the reasons why a large number of animals are not imitated by artists. For example, why does the monkey in Chinese paintings always hold a peach? Why is only the spotted sika deer depicted in paintings? And why is the owl not seen in Chinese art? All of these are fascinating. Mr. Su's lecture will trace back to the pictographs and bones of the Shang Dynasty 3,000 years ago, down to the most recent modern times, and will use specimens, rubbings, and lantern slides from his personal collection to aid in the explanation.

One Hundred and Fifteen Patients in One Week

The Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road began displaying a monitor lizard yesterday. At the same time, the Pigeon Research Association, affiliated with the zoo, has scheduled a pigeon race for the eighth of next month. Details are as follows:

The zoo began displaying a large lizard (commonly known as a monitor lizard) in the aquarium room yesterday. From head to tail, it is four feet long, with a gray-brown back and belly. Pigeon Race

Special Committee Meeting of National Medicine Organizations 167

Discussing the Monopoly of Wolfberries

The Shanghai Traditional Chinese Medicine Trade Association, due to the price of wolfberries rising sharply more than threefold this year while the quality has deteriorated, conducted detailed investigations and discovered that ambitious individuals, repeating the mistakes of ivory monopolies, have formed organizations to manipulate the market for profit. The current market price is just a small taste of their success. The association, considering the matter serious, sent a letter to the Tianjin Yu Ning Company questioning the reasons for the price increase. After more than a month with no response, the association convened a special committee meeting of traditional Chinese medicine organizations at 7:00 PM on the 13th of this month in the association's meeting room. Xie Liheng of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association, He Yunsheng of the Shanghai Traditional Chinese Medicine Society, Shi Jiqun of the China Traditional Chinese Medicine Society, Li Kangnian, Song Fuchen, Tao Ran, Yuan Pinzhang, and Shen Hefu of the Traditional Chinese Medicine Trade Association attended. Chaired by Xie Liheng, the meeting resolved: (1) Medical organizations will jointly send another letter to Yu Ning Company, questioning the reasons for the price increase. (2) Appeal to Chairman Ma of Ningxia to order the company not to hoard and raise prices, preventing the monopolization of medicines, and request the Central Traditional Chinese Medicine Museum to consult Chairman Ma to uphold justice. (3) and (4) Simultaneously, the special committee decided to edit a unified nomenclature of medicines, with two representatives from the Traditional Chinese Medicine Association, the China Medical Association, the Shenzhou Medical Association, and the Shanghai Traditional Chinese Medicine Society, and five representatives from the Traditional Chinese Medicine Trade Association forming a committee to be responsible for this task, aiming to complete this work in a short period.

Shanghai County Uses Baojia System to Ban Opium 169

YWCA Board Meeting Resolutions 173

The Shanghai YWCA at No. 999 Jing'an Temple Road held a board meeting at 9:00 AM on the 13th. Attendees included Mrs. He Lin Yi, Mrs. Ling Xian Yang, Mrs. Song Xing Cun, Mrs. Mei Hua Quan, Mrs. Huang Xi En, Mrs. Ying Chen Tao, Mrs. Huang Shu Pei, Ms. Xia Ma Li, Mrs. Dong Xian Guang, General Secretary Ms. Xie Zu Yi, Secretary Ms. Zhang Zhi Xue, and others.
